Commentary

Austrian Rearmament and the European Situation

— A Cold Observation

A Vienna dispatch reported a few days ago that the Austrian government has issued a statement planning to immediately reinstate conscription and begin preparations to increase the army to 65,000 men. It also intends to send a special envoy to participate in the Stresa Conference on the 11th of this month (the conference of England, France, and Italy), requesting the great powers to allow it. Hungary and Bulgaria also intend to request the same, following suit. Although the steps taken are different from Germany's outright abandonment of the treaty, it is quite obvious that Austria is unwilling to be bound by the Treaty of Saint-Germain. The Treaty of Saint-Germain was the treaty between various countries and Austria after the Great War, signed on September 10, 1919, in the Château de Saint-Germain-en-Laye, southeast of Paris. According to Article 4 of the treaty, restrictions on Austrian armaments were very strict, such as the total number of the army not exceeding 30,000 men, and the abolition of conscription forever. This was exactly the same as the intention of the Treaty of Versailles to restrict German armaments. Germany has already rearmed, officially establishing an air force on April 1. Hitler himself admitted that the strength of his country's air force is comparable to that of Britain. This was due to secret arrangements made in advance and relentless progress according to a predetermined plan, until preparations were complete before openly announcing it. Now Austria has also announced its rearmament, using Germany's actions as an excuse. Since Germany has freely shaken off the constraints of the Treaty of Versailles, Austria no longer needs to be restricted by the Treaty of Saint-Germain. The authorities of the two countries defend themselves, saying that the actions of the great powers today prioritize strengthening their military power, and they cannot solely blame Germany and Austria for abiding by the treaty. Their arguments are not without merit.

Consequently, recent speculation about the future of peace in Europe is varied and inconclusive. Generally speaking, there are two schools of thought: pessimistic and optimistic. Pessimists believe that the rearmament of Germany and Austria, one after the other, is a sign of the eve of the Second World War. Since the September 18th Incident, the League of Nations has been unable to sanction Japan, and the covenant is merely a formality. Now Germany and Austria have torn up the Treaties of Paris, and the great powers can do nothing about it. In the future, international disputes will have no way to be resolved except by resorting to force. Existing treaties will become waste paper. There are also so-called Central European Pacts and Eastern European Pacts, which are being discussed and implemented. Those who violate agreements and betray trust can act with impunity. Even if new treaties are concluded, it will be in vain. The internal contradictions of imperialism will always exist, and the opportunity for bloody conflict cannot be avoided. The great powers glare at each other, tensions are high, and the outbreak of the Second World War is not far off. However, optimists say that this is not entirely true. When hostilities broke out in August 1914, Germany relied on its well-equipped army and allied support, and Ning was the leader of the war. But now times have changed. Germany has fallen into a state of isolation. Although it has violated its vows and rearmed, it may not be able to regain its power in Europe. Moreover, its old ally, Austria, is apprehensive day and night, fearing annexation by Germany. This declaration to reinstate conscription, nominally a request to follow suit, is actually a strict precaution against Germany. In diplomatic terms, it has obtained the understanding of France, so the Austrian authorities are confident and resolute in taking this step. On January 7 of this year, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval signed the Rome Accords. On February 3, Laval and British Foreign Secretary Simon issued the London Declaration. These people have done their best to avoid war and protect European security. The Soviet Union is close to France, and France is allied with Britain and Italy. Their common intention to counter Germany is clearly visible. Even if Germany fully restores its military strength to its former state, how dare it rashly provoke war and repeat its mistakes? As for the attitude of the British authorities, they have always advocated amending the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles. Some say that this is protecting Germany, but this is not entirely true. Germany has been deliberately unwilling to be bound by the Treaty of Versailles. Not only the British, but also other countries' authorities have long been aware of this. Its military reorganization has been going on for a long time, and it was only recently publicly announced. Since other countries cannot stop it, it is useless to leave restrictions on paper. Therefore, the London Declaration proposes to amend the military clauses. British dignitaries like Eden have been traveling between Moscow, Warsaw, and Berlin, working tirelessly to maintain the balance of power in Europe. According to recent reports from London, Eden's visit to Moscow was met with quite close discussions. The House of Commons does not urgently request the government to explain the situation of negotiations with the Soviet Union, and the majority party is already showing goodwill. From this, it can be inferred that Britain's attitude is to increase friendship with the Soviet Union. It is neither anti-Soviet nor pro-German. The only difference between its attitude towards Germany and that of France is that it is more moderate. In short, European powers such as Britain, the Soviet Union, France, and Italy are not only doing their best to strengthen their military power, but also mediating for peace in order to avoid war. Austria's release from the bonds of the Treaty of Saint-Germain and its request for the great powers to allow it are different from Germany's outright abandonment of the treaty. It is still uncertain whether the European situation will not break down, but it is unlikely that war will break out in the near future.

Both of the above arguments can be justified and have some basis. We do not need to force a judgment. Judging from the current efforts of all parties to pursue peace, the optimistic view seems more powerful. However, considering the fanaticism of various countries in expanding their military power and the increasingly tense international situation, the pessimistic view has strong reasons. However, there are two points that must be pointed out. First, the instability and unease of the European situation are obvious facts that no one can deny. Second, whether the European situation will not break down is something that no one dares to guarantee. With these two points clear, our countrymen should realize that trouble in Europe is not a blessing for China. If our country is still in the memory of the Eastern oppression it suffered during the First World War, then before the Second World War comes, our countrymen should be vigilant and make preparations in advance.

Page 6

To Soothe the European Situation, Britain Plans to Open a New Path: To Abandon the Eastern European Security Pact; The Opinions of the Three Countries are Diametrically Opposed; The Stresa Conference Opens on Thursday; It is Decided that the Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Will Participate

(London) It was learned tonight that the cabinet has a tendency to abandon the Eastern European Security Pact and open a new path to achieve an agreement. The so-called "new route" should be formed at tomorrow's cabinet meeting. The government now believes that the Eastern European Pact contains clauses on military assistance, which have now been aborted due to the opposition of Germany and Poland to the participation of Soviet Russia. In view of this situation, Britain is gradually advocating that it is unwilling to participate in any mutual assistance agreement other than the Western European Pact. If France and Russia disregard Germany and conclude this Eastern European Pact on their own, Britain can only stand by. According to a Paris dispatch, Britain's attitude has increased the frustration of people in the French capital, because the French authorities believe that the opinions of Britain, France, and Italy are diametrically opposed, which is enough to endanger the Stresa Conference. According to news from here, Britain is willing to see the non-aggression treaty extended to the European continent, but it is unwilling to be drawn into the whirlpool of war. The military alliance of France, Russia, and Czechoslovakia may take a sharp turn for the worse. These three countries also hope that Estonia, Latvia, and Lithuania will act in unison. Germany is recuperating, quietly watching the changes, and believes that after its strength is sufficient, it will not worry about having allies. (National Telegram on the 7th)

(London) Prime Minister MacDonald announced in the House of Commons tonight that he and Foreign Secretary Simon will participate in the Stresa Conference. The conference is scheduled to open on April 11. (Reuters Telegram on the 8th)

Cabinet Listens to Report

(London) This morning, the cabinet held a special meeting to discuss the detailed records and personal impressions of the talks with the authorities during Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden's visits to several European capitals, which lasted for two hours. Then, the people who will attend the Stresa Conference were decided. Simon will make a brief statement in the House of Commons today, and plans to make a longer general statement tomorrow.

Eden Absent Due to Illness

Eden was unable to attend the cabinet meeting today due to excessive fatigue from the trip. According to a bulletin issued by his medical advisor today, Eden's mind is restless due to excessive fatigue from recent air travel. His condition is not a cause for concern, but he must rest for four to six weeks. The British government and the public were concerned when they heard the news of Eden's illness. Prime Minister MacDonald visited him and said that he was worried about Eden's illness for both public and private reasons. Currently, telegrams are pouring in from all over the world wishing Eden a speedy recovery, many of whom are friends he met on this trip. Simon and Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs Vansittart visited Eden on Saturday and Sunday. On Sunday, the Prime Minister also visited him to discuss the results of the visits to various countries. Since taking office as Lord Privy Seal last year, Eden has traveled thousands of miles by air, land, and sea. He has visited Geneva five times, and has been to Paris, Rome, and Berlin for disarmament issues. He has also reciprocated visits to Denmark, Norway, and Sweden. (Reuters Telegram on the 8th)

(Paris) Lord Privy Seal Eden of Britain has visited Germany, Russia, Poland, and Czechoslovakia, and after returning to Britain, he has fallen slightly ill. He cannot attend the cabinet meeting today and will not go to the Stresa Conference. The Paris Echo newspaper regrets this news. The newspaper also learned that the British government will be represented by Prime Minister MacDonald at the Stresa Conference. According to a report from the London Daily News, this matter has been confirmed and will be decided at today's British cabinet meeting. Therefore, the Paris Echo said that since the British Prime Minister is participating in person, Premier Flandin should also attend, because it is necessary for the British, French, and Italian government authorities to discuss everything face-to-face at the Stresa Conference. (Havas Telegram on the 8th)

French Communist Party Representative Selection Decided at Today's Cabinet Meeting

(Paris) The Stresa Conference of Britain, France, and Italy is about to be held. Regarding the selection of representatives from France, according to responsible parties, in addition to Foreign Minister Laval deciding to attend in person, Premier Flandin may also go, but the final decision will be made after tomorrow's cabinet meeting. (Havas Telegram on the 8th) A "Certain Times" newspaper commented on the European situation, saying, "There are now three possible steps: first, cooperate with Germany; second, unite to defend against Germany; and third, a messy front with unclear responsibilities. One of the above three must be clearly chosen. The newspaper believes that the Stresa Conference should be the final solution, but if various covenants are signed to cover up the situation, it will inevitably fall into a magic circle, create a bad atmosphere, and fail to achieve a practical solution. The danger of this is extreme. There are also many strategies being attempted now. One group advocates signing bilateral covenants to oppose regional covenants, while another advocates general covenants with safeguards and sanctions to oppose covenants without sanctions. However, in any case, adopting a middle-ground solution is better than allowing a chaotic and uneasy atmosphere to continue to prolong." (Havas Telegram on the 8th)

British Diplomatic Strategy: Expected to Be No More Than Two Paths

(London) All newspapers attach great importance to today's cabinet meeting, believing that its resolutions are extremely relevant to British foreign policy. The newspapers regret that Lord Privy Seal Eden cannot attend the cabinet meeting to report on his visits to Germany, Russia, Poland, and Czechoslovakia. The Morning Post said, "The problem that should be solved now is whether Britain should continue to be a mediator between the European powers, or decisively decide to join one side of the opponents of amending the treaty." The newspaper believes that it is not impossible to seek a compromise with Germany, but to establish a final coordination, it will take many years. If there are no better guarantees at present to prevent the National Socialist Party from taking reckless actions again, then the actions of the great powers to resist Germany with force are inevitable. The London Daily News has a similar view, saying that British foreign policy is no more than two paths: one is to maintain the current state of isolation, which is neither glorious nor sustainable, and the other is to resolutely assist in collective action under the leadership of the League of Nations. Which of these two paths Britain will choose is the key to the future peace of Europe. The majority of British cabinet members agree with the principle of collective action, because only collective action can prevent the outbreak of war in the present and future. The Times said that Britain is unwilling to engage in war, but Britain should express its firm opposition to those who engage in war. Moreover, Britain must find ways to eliminate the current uneasy situation in the international community so that the latent roots of war can be completely eliminated. The newspaper also said that there is no danger of any aggression at present. The goal of British diplomatic efforts is to make Germany join the collective peace system and the League of Nations. The Daily Herald said that if one of the three, the British-French-Italian Pact, the Eastern European Pact, or the Western European Pact, is missing, there is no way to generate a sense of peace. To ensure peace in Europe, it is necessary to first increase the strength of Geneva, and then start discussing the amendment of the treaty. (Havas Telegram on the 8th)

French Foreign Minister Will Succeed Eden in Visiting the Capitals of Russia and Poland; Departure Scheduled for the 23rd of This Month; Discussing the Situation Caused by German Rearmament

(Paris) According to news from here today, French Foreign Minister Laval will visit Warsaw at the invitation of Poland, but will first go to Moscow. The purpose of this trip is to discuss ways to alleviate the serious situation caused by Germany's decision to rearm. Laval will leave Paris for Moscow on April 23 and will stay in the Russian capital for about three days before going to Warsaw. (Reuters Telegram on the 8th)

Italy Is Willing to Join Hands With Southern Countries to Oppose the Forcible Amendment of the Treaty

The newly appointed Italian ambassador to Yugoslavia's capital, Gambardo, recently gave an interview to the Truth newspaper, saying, "Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has the best intentions towards Yugoslavia and is willing to establish a lasting compromise with the southern country. If there are disputes between the two countries, they should be resolved. For example, the two countries have signed several agreements, but they have not been implemented for various reasons. After this is resolved, a new commercial treaty should be signed and a friendly treaty should be prepared, or the existing friendly treaty should be extended." Gambardo further explained that the late King Alexander I of the Southern Kingdom and the late French Foreign Minister Barthou also supported Italy and the Southern Kingdom working together, and said, "Italy recognizes the Little Entente as a good international organization with the ability to survive and political ideas. As for the issue of amending the treaty, Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant has already stated that international treaties can be amended, but they must be carried out through legal procedures. Italy has always opposed forcibly amending it." (Havas Telegram on the 7th)

People in Paris Donate to Build a Memorial for the Late King of the South

(Paris) A public fundraising was held here today to build a memorial for the former King Alexander I of Yugoslavia. The government specially allowed this day to be a national fundraising day. Foreign Minister Laval also gave a wireless radio speech last night, asking the people of France to contribute generously. From this morning, male and female team members in Paris streets, with tricolor national emblems wrapped around their arms, were asking passers-by to donate. All donors were given a badge to wear on their chest to show their recognition. The badge depicts a portrait of King Alexander of the South, surrounded by a wreath, with a Yugoslav flag painted on top. (Havas Telegram on the 7th)

Following in Germany's Footsteps, Austria, Hungary, and Bulgaria Will Demand Military Expansion; Britain and Italy Tend to Support It; The Restoration of Austria Is Temporarily Deferred

(Rome) The Italian People's Newspaper, which has a semi-official nature, hinted today that the Italian government is willing to support any action by Austria, Hungary, and Bulgaria to expand their armies. The newspaper discussed the level of armaments of the three countries, saying that it is a crime that violates any principle of international equality that strong countries like Germany are allowed to unilaterally rearm, while weak countries are not allowed to have this right. Italy's attitude on this matter will be stated at the Stresa Conference. (Reuters Telegram on the 7th)

(Rome) The semi-official "Italian People's Newspaper" published an article discussing the increase in armaments of Austria, Hungary, and Bulgaria, stating, "Why not generously acknowledge the military clauses of the treaty that were unilaterally decided to be abolished, based on justice? The treaty should be amended by those responsible for peace as an act of reconciliation, so that on the one hand, the treaty is not openly violated, and on the other hand, violent protests are not made. If the military clauses in the treaty are amended in a friendly spirit, then the distinction between the victorious and defeated countries can be completely eliminated, and the relationship between the three countries of Austria, Hungary, and Bulgaria and the Little Entente will inevitably be improved." (Havas Telegram on the 8th)

(Vienna) Austria is very excited today, and the public's attention has once again focused on the possibility of a Habsburg royal restoration. Officials still deny that Austria's request to the great powers to allow it to double its army is aimed at preparing for Archduke Otto to ascend the throne. However, rumors have spread on the borders of Romania and Yugoslavia, and it has been announced that the Little Entente will do its utmost to oppose the amendment of the Treaty of Saint-Germain, which stipulates that Austria's army is currently only allowed to have 30,000 long-term volunteer soldiers. Austria has announced that it will send representatives to the Stresa Conference to request a doubling of the military quota and to implement conscription. Italy has expressed its support for the plan, and Britain has expressed its agreement if Austria can abide by the Treaty of Saint-Germain. Bulgaria and Hungary have also requested to increase their military strength, saying that the surrounding countries are all strong in military equipment, and their military strength is weak, making it difficult for them to defend themselves. As for Austrian Prime Minister Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Woudenegg, they are both pro-imperialist figures, but because of the opposition of other countries and their unwillingness to offend Britain and France, they have not yet tried to have Archduke Otto ascend the throne. The Austrian Prime Minister once said that if the National Socialist Party does not plan to seize power, he will not resort to the restoration route. At present, Archduke Otto and his mother are still living in the suburbs of Brussels. It is said that economic problems are the biggest obstacle to the current restoration movement. Austria is unable to support a monarch, because if Otto ascends the throne, more than 200 impoverished archdukes and archduchesses will return to the country with him, and they all need to be supported by the state. The cost is shocking. After the war, Austria was a beggar country in Europe, and its living resources were subject to the treaty. Therefore, the pain it suffered from the treaty was more than that of other countries. Therefore, Britain and Italy deeply feel that Austria should be rewarded. According to observers, regardless of whether the Stresa Conference can allow Austria to rearm, Archduke Otto has no hope of restoration for the time being, because if the Habsburg royal family is restored without the consent of the Little Entente, war may follow within a short time. As for why the Little Entente opposes it, there are various reasons. After the restoration, Austria will be easier to unify and become stronger. Therefore, the Catholic people of the Little Entente will also seek to establish a monarch of the Habsburg royal family in their respective countries. Moreover, the Slavic people of the Czech Republic, the Croat people of Yugoslavia, and the Transylvanian people of Romania are all Catholics and may be drawn to Austria. It is heard that the great powers such as Britain, France, and Italy are no longer very opposed to the restoration of Austria. The leaders of the three countries all believe that after Austria restores the imperial system, it may be able to contain Hitler's ambitions in Central and Southern Europe. If the great powers do not oppose it, it is only a matter of time before the Little Entente changes its attitude. (National Telegram on the 8th)

Austrian Army Grand Review: The Prime Minister Exhorts the Soldiers to Work Together to Fight for Independence

(Vienna) The Austrian Army held a grand review ceremony today. Prime Minister Schuschnigg delivered a speech, hoping that the Austrian Army would恪遵the example of the late Prime Minister Dollfuss, that is, work together to fight for Austria's independence, happiness, and rights. (Havas Telegram on the 7th)

The Austrian Situation Is Tense Again: The Storm Troopers and the Home Guard Are at Odds; The Two Extremist Factions Are Taking Advantage of the Opportunity to Stir Up Trouble Again

(Vienna) The Austrian situation is tense again today, because the government's two major private armies, namely Prime Minister Schuschnigg's Storm Troopers and Prince Starhemberg's Home Guard, are at odds. The National Socialist Party and the Communist Party are taking advantage of the opportunity to stir up trouble again. As for the jealousy between the Storm Troopers and the Home Guard, it is mainly due to the fact that one side plans to squeeze Starhemberg to be the regent. Starhemberg's regency is only a transition for the Habsburg restoration. The two armies recently clashed in small towns. There are also rumors in Vienna that Prime Minister Schuschnigg is tired of his job and that the fascism he is pursuing is nearing its end. (National Telegram on the 7th)

The Whole of Germany Flies Flags Today to Celebrate the Birthday of the Great General of the European War

(Berlin) The German leader Hitler ordered all agencies across the country to fly flags on the 9th of this month to celebrate the 70th birthday of General Ludendorff, the great general of Germany during the European War. The order stated, "In order to commemorate the general's achievements, we should all raise flags to pay tribute on the 9th of this month." (National Telegram on the 8th)

The Result of the Danzig Parliament Re-election: The German Nazi Party's Long-Held Wish Unfulfilled; Fails to Obtain Two-Thirds of the Votes; Constitutional Amendment Dreams Dashed

Danzig: The preliminary results of the city council elections are as follows: Nazi Party 139,729 votes (in the May 1933 elections, it was 109,729 votes); Social Democratic Party 37,015 votes (previously 37,882 votes); Communist Party 7,990 votes (previously 14,566 votes); Catholic Center Party 31,525 votes (previously 31,336 votes); German National People's Party 9,691 votes (previously 13,596 votes); Polish people 8,130 votes (previously 6,743 votes); Veterans Opposition 385 votes.

In summary, the Nazi Party's obtained votes do not reach 60% of the total. (Havas Dispatch, 8th)

Danzig: The Nazi Party is greatly disappointed with the results of yesterday's election. According to the latest figures, the number of seats held by each party in the new parliament is as follows:

Nazi Party 44, Social Democratic Party 12, Center Party 9, German National People's Party 3, Communist Party and Polish Party 2 each. The Nazi Party only gained four more seats than last time. Dr. Rauschning, who served as the Administrative President of Danzig from July 1933 until his resignation in 1934, fled the area today, presumably to Poland. It is said that the Nazi Party regards him as a traitor and intends to harm him. German Propaganda Minister Goebbels said in a speech on Saturday that the Nazi Party should not pay attention to people like Rauschning because he has already committed spiritual suicide. (Reuters Dispatch, 8th)

Danzig: In yesterday's election for the new parliament in Danzig, despite the German propaganda machine's all-out efforts to obtain a two-thirds majority in order to petition the League of Nations to change the constitution of the Free City, the result was only a three-fifths majority. The total number of votes obtained by the Nazi Party this time was approximately 30,000 more than in the previous election in 1933.

During the vote count, the representative of the Polish government in Danzig stated that the Germans had used terror tactics during the election and that it should be considered illegal. According to a note from the representative to the Danzig authorities, two Polish employees in his office were beaten up early yesterday morning and should be compensated for their losses. Voting began at 9:00 AM yesterday, and approximately 25% of the people went to the polling stations. By the afternoon, 70% of the voters had cast their ballots. On that day, flags flew throughout the city, and various parties held demonstrations in the city center. However, apart from the beating of the two Polish employees, no other incidents occurred. The German government provided travel expenses to 6,000 Danzig citizens and arranged special transportation to bring them to vote. It also sent capable personnel such as Hess, a confidant of the German leader, Gauleiter Bruckner of Saar, Propaganda Minister Goebbels, and Prussian President Göring to campaign, expecting to obtain a two-thirds majority in order to change the constitution of the Free City and break away from the protection of the League of Nations. Unexpectedly, their wish was not fulfilled. (Reuters Dispatch, 8th)

(Paris) The newspapers believe that this election of the Danzig Free City Council, although heavily promoted by the German Nazi Party, can be considered a partial failure or a partial success when its results are compared with the 1933 elections. Le Petit Parisien reported, "If this failure is finally confirmed, it will inevitably cause a profound reaction on the German side and be regarded as the first defeat of Nazism. If Germany wants to amend the current constitution of Danzig City according to legal procedures and merge the Danzig City administration with the German administration, the Nazi Party must obtain two-thirds of the total votes to succeed. In addition, some political circles are deeply concerned that if the election results disappoint Germany, the Nazi Party may stage a military coup." The newspaper also stated, "The Nazi Party's major propaganda efforts and sudden victory were due to unity and organization. The Nazi Party's small victory this time is particularly frightening because it will cause the German government's oppressive policies to continue unabated." L'Écho de Paris stated, "The League of Nations should pay more attention to the current system of Danzig City than in the past. The League of Nations should especially remember the words of German Propaganda Minister Goebbels yesterday that Danzig City will sooner or later fall into the arms of Germany because this statement is nothing short of a provocative act against the League of Nations and at the same time a serious warning to Poland." (Havas Dispatch, 8th)

New Japanese Military Attaché to China: Isotani Will Come to China Soon

They left after an hour. Mr. Hobbes also visited former Foreign Minister Shidehara at his private residence at 5:00 PM in the afternoon. (Rengo Dispatch, 8th)

The American side was represented by the entire team, led by Team Leader Hobbes. International Commerce—Reuters Special Business Intelligence Telegram for April 8th

Gold and Silver

The price of gold in London soared again this morning, listed at 144 shillings and 11 pence, 10 pence higher than Saturday. This is due to the easing of the pound sterling.

The London silver market was quite volatile today before listing. It was predicted that it would rise by 0.0625, but the listed price for spot was 28 pence 4375, the same as the previous price, while futures were 28 pence 5625, up 0.0625. India and China were both buying and selling in the morning. The closing price was stable.

The Bombay silver market was also calm today. The opening price for spot was 68 rupees, 2 annas higher than the closing price on Saturday. There was no change until 12:15, and the market was lackluster.

Exchange Rates

British-American The rise in the price of gold national currency at the close of trading on Saturday, which was caused by the increased trust in the gold national currency's ability to protect its currency, has not subsided this morning. However, the foreign exchange market is generally quite quiet. Operators who rushed to exchange their gold coins for pounds sterling at the end of last week are no longer as panicked as before, so the demand for pounds sterling has eased slightly. For this reason, the pound sterling is now weak in terms of gold coins and US dollars. The opening exchange rate between British and American was $4.8225, 0.125 lower than the closing price of the US-British exchange rate on Saturday. There was a slight improvement in the morning, but it stagnated slightly at noon. The price at 2:00 PM in the afternoon was $4.83125, 0.875 higher than the opening. The market was relatively quiet. Also, one US dollar is equivalent to four shillings and one penny 676 in British gold.

British-French The opening price was 73 francs 15, 50 points lower than the closing price on Saturday. It rose slightly at 11:00, but returned to the opening price at noon. The price jumped up 10 points at 2:00 PM in the afternoon to 73 francs 25.

US-British The pound sterling fell slightly today. The opening exchange rate between US and British was $4.83125, down 0.125. The fluctuations were narrow, and the market was calm.

US-French The rise in gold coins on Saturday reappeared slightly today. The opening exchange rate between US and French was $6.59375, 0.375 higher than the closing price on Saturday.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton The cotton market opened about 5 points higher, but within the first hour, almost all of the gains were lost, and the market turned quiet with very sluggish trading. The currency price fluctuations seemed to be subsiding, and one element of manipulating the market price in the cotton market was thus eliminated. In terms of weather, there was rain in the eastern cotton belt, but it was not what the cotton farmers needed. The pressure of counter-donation is now increasing daily. There are rumors that someone has advised the president to exercise his privileges to abolish this donation.

Chicago Wheat The opening was about one point higher. The market price of grain in Winnipeg rose, and the dry area narrowed. However, the statistical position is conducive to higher prices.

Liverpool Cotton Today there is a more stable trend. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, the asking price for July futures was 6.13, 6 points higher than the closing price on Saturday.

Liverpool Wheat The market price was slightly lower today because those who profited from the price increase on Saturday sold off, and the Chicago wheat market also fell at the close of trading on Saturday. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, the price for July futures was 5 shillings and 7 pence, 0.125 lower than on Saturday.

Bombay Cotton Market The price rose slightly today, but the market was quiet. The price of Bai Luozhi cotton for July-August futures was 222 rupees, 2 rupees higher than on Saturday. This price did not move before noon.

Rubber

London The opening was stable today, with prices the same as the closing price on Saturday, but the atmosphere was weaker before noon. At noon, the transaction price for July-September futures was 5 pence 5 holes 25, down 0.0625. The market was quiet after the price fell.

New York The opening today fell by 20 points due to the drop in prices in London. Within half an hour of the opening, the downward trend did not stop. The rubber market seems to be entirely controlled by foreign markets. Although various domestic markets are now strong, they have no impact on the rubber market. Merchants are all taking a wait-and-see attitude.

Securities

New York Except for the considerable pressure on railway stocks and retail sales of public utility stocks, the general price of the securities market this morning was higher than before. The atmosphere turned better at the opening, and the market was firm. The resistance to profit-taking discovered on Saturday has made the foothold more stable. Today, everyone feels that if there is any news that is slightly beneficial to the market, it can promote an upward trend in prices, but there is no exciting general news. Within half an hour of the opening, the pressure on railway and public utility stocks no longer existed. The slight increase at the opening gradually expanded and rose by one or two points. The market is still active, and the atmosphere is also stable. The New York securities market prices are listed on the left:

Severe Wind Disaster in the Southern United States: The Town of Crossroads Completely Destroyed; Thousands Left Homeless

Jackson, Mississippi: A hurricane struck Mississippi and Louisiana today, killing 33 people, seriously injuring 200, and leaving thousands homeless, with tens of millions of dollars in property damage. Among the 33 deaths, 10 were people who went boating on the Mississippi River at the end of the week and encountered a storm. The boat capsized in the middle of the river, and all were drowned. The small town of Crossroads, with a population of 1,200, was completely destroyed, killing 12 and injuring 100, with serious injuries. The hurricane blew down church spires, houses, warehouses, and other three-dimensional buildings, broke trees, telegraph and telephone lines, and cut off electricity. More than a dozen other small towns were also severely damaged. Most parts of the state and Louisiana were affected by the wind disaster. The state's Red Cross and other charitable organizations quickly mobilized, earning the praise of the people. Airplanes, trains, and cars loaded with food, tents, medicine, doctors, and nurses rushed to Crossroads and other disaster areas. As of now, 33 deaths have been learned of here, but the number of deaths will inevitably increase greatly after reports from all parties are gathered. (National Telegraph, 7th)

Hurricane Passes Through the Philippines: Trees Uprooted, Houses Collapsed, and Transportation Disrupted

(Manila) Southern Luzon still has a hurricane today, with 4 deaths and thousands of houses destroyed. Samar and Leyte provinces had the strongest winds, and it is reported that 1,000 houses were blown down in Albay province. Details of the disaster are still lacking due to transportation disruptions. Roads everywhere are blocked by fallen trees and telephone poles. (National Telegraph, 8th)

Devaluation of Dutch and Swiss Currencies: Only a Matter of Time

(London) After the Dutch authorities tried their best to protect the Dutch guilder, short sellers covered their positions in advance, causing the Dutch and Swiss currencies to rise. However, it is the general opinion here today that the Netherlands and Switzerland will eventually follow in the footsteps of Belgium and reduce the value of their currencies. This is only a matter of time because the currencies of these two countries are very vulnerable to attack due to their weak economic situation. If the Dutch guilder is devalued, what will happen to rubber? It is expected that the Dutch government will take this opportunity to levy an export tax on the Dutch East Indies. A rubber industry expert said that if the Dutch currency is devalued, the price of rubber from the natives of the Dutch East Indies will inevitably be high, and the production of native rubber will inevitably increase greatly. Therefore, the authorities should increase the existing export tax in proportion to the degree of currency devaluation. This method must be implemented immediately after the currency is devalued. The Dutch guilder has only a temporary impact on rubber because rubber is actually tied to US consumption in the summer and autumn, and the amount of US consumption will depend on the outcome of the US employment case. (Reuters Dispatch, 8th)

1934: Record Flow of Gold to the United States; Two Reasons

(Washington) According to a statement released by the Department of Commerce today, the flow of gold into the United States in 1934 created a new record. There are two reasons for the huge influx of gold into the United States: (1) Funds exported in 1933 were returned to the country, (2) Exports exceeded imports by $478,000,000 in 1934. Government experts said that the political situation in some gold bloc countries is unstable, and they have transported cash here to seek safety. Therefore, there is a huge amount of gold imported into the United States. The total value of gold imported in 1934 was $1,187,000,000, and the value of gold exported was only $53,000,000, a net increase of $1,134,000,000. The report also stated that the total value of silver imported into the United States in 1934 was $103,000,000, and the value of silver exported was $17,000,000, a net increase of $86,000,000. (National Telegraph, 7th)

Ministry of Finance Urges Provinces to Abolish Onerous Taxes

(Nanjing) A certain official of the Ministry of Finance said that the situation in each province regarding the abolition of onerous taxes is quite inconsistent. There are indeed many provinces that have fully complied, but there are still a small number of provinces that have not been able to achieve this on schedule. For the sake of supervision, the government intends to formulate restrictive measures. Provinces that completely abolish onerous taxes will be allocated 40% of the stamp tax revenue each month according to the amount. Otherwise, the allocation will be temporarily suspended. Recently, a small number of local authorities have complained that the designated subsidies have not been issued. It is not known that the central government's subsidies are safely stored in the national treasury. If the local authorities abolish the taxes quickly, they will be able to quickly obtain them, which is not a problem. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

Ministry of Finance Tentatively Drafts Measures to Unify Paper Money

(Nanjing) In order to unify the paper money in each province, the Ministry of Finance has drafted measures for exchange notes. Before the measures are formally drafted and announced, three provisional measures are proposed: (1) Provincial banks or local banks shall not issue exchange notes of one yuan or more, and shall use the exchange notes of the Central Bank. (2) In order to regulate rural finance, various auxiliary currency notes of less than one yuan will be temporarily issued by provincial banks or local banks. 60% of the reserve cash should be prepared, and 40% of the guarantee money should be prepared, but 20% of the cash can be replaced by warehouse receipts. (3) If provincial banks or local banks have already issued exchange notes of one yuan or more, the Ministry of Finance will investigate the amount and order them to be withdrawn. Before the withdrawal, the exchange notes of the Central Bank will be used as reserve funds and handed over to the Central Bank for safekeeping. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

Judicial Yuan Interpretation of Ambiguities in the Age Characteristics of the Criminal Procedure Law

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan's interpretation of the ambiguities in Article 258 of the Criminal Procedure Law is as follows: The defendant's age and other characteristics that can be used to identify him do not necessarily have to be known to the victim. The omission of the defendant's age and characteristics in the indictment alone cannot be used as a reason to reject it on the grounds that the prosecution procedure violates the regulations. After Chairman Chiang Arrived in Guizhou, Guiyang Took on a New Look. The Central Army Implemented the New Life Movement. Chairman Chiang Strove for Construction and Industry.

A Guiyang dispatch from the Zi Lin Daily on April 1st states that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and his wife arrived here by plane on March 24th, greatly exciting the local officials and attracting the attention of the people. In recent years, no high-ranking officials of the central government have visited Guizhou. Now that such an important figure has arrived, the entire city is decorated with flags and banners to express welcome. Moreover, because Chairman Chiang is the advocate of the New Life Movement, the entire city has been cleaned and renovated in recent days, taking on a new look.

When the communist bandits were not far from the provincial capital and the provincial army was plotting to loot the entire city and retreat the next day, the central army suddenly arrived, and the local area was saved from danger. At first, the shops were half-closed, and the shopkeepers secretly hid their valuables, waiting for the disaster to descend. Unexpectedly, a savior arrived, and they were as happy and excited as schoolchildren. The provincial army was particularly displeased, as it missed a great opportunity. From then on, the shops were fully open, the streets were thoroughly cleaned, and the atmosphere completely changed. The central army also took on the role of street police, and their treatment of the people was kind, unlike any previous soldiers. The New Life Movement was immediately launched in the army, and people in specially made uniforms were sent to guide the people on the streets. These people did not carry weapons, only batons, but they did not strike the backs of the ignorant villagers.

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has patrolled the city many times and consulted with various senior officials, paying attention to the overall situation in the province. The province is permeated with opium smoke, and many people are addicted to opium. Chairman Chiang is now eager to eliminate this scourge, but during conversations, he expressed that the habit is deeply ingrained and that unless farmers are first helped to change to other crops and addicts are helped to quit, it is impossible to suddenly issue a ban on planting and smoking. He later stated during a conversation that the urgent task today is to completely change the nation's concept of employing people and engaging in productive work. In other words, it is necessary to develop natural resources and improve agriculture.

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek always pursues a policy of building roads and developing remote areas, and it is the same when he arrives here. Chiang ordered in Chongqing to complete the highways from Chongqing to northern Guizhou and from Changsha to Guizhou as soon as possible. Roads are currently being built here to the north of the province to connect with Chongqing. Chiang also believes that it is now urgent to develop small industries to utilize natural products. About eighty or ninety miles from here, there is a 300-foot-high waterfall, which can be used to generate electricity to supply the entire province. Although Guiyang has a small power plant, electricity is only available from 7:00 PM to 12:00 AM every night, and only a few intersections in the city are equipped with electric lights. The rest of the roads and most of the residences are dark at night. In addition, transportation is difficult, and the price of kerosene is extremely high. Ordinary people cannot afford to buy it, so as soon as it gets dark, every family closes their doors and goes to bed, and there are few people on the road. The province is rich in coal, but it contains sulfur. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek knows that this is a type of industry that can be developed, as it can supply the grease used for road construction, or even refined into gasoline, and its by-products can be used to make pigments. Chiang also feels that it is now appropriate to purchase chemical fertilizers on a large scale to increase agricultural production, and to use barren mountains for animal husbandry. The Miao people are quite knowledgeable in this area, so their cattle and sheep thrive. Chiang's flight here has made him deeply aware of the difficulties of traveling here, so he intends to prioritize the development of transportation. In the past, traveling by bridge from Chongqing to here took seventeen days. Now, by plane, it only takes two hours. When the highway is built, if it remains flat, it will only take two days to arrive. The province is extremely rich in minerals, but they are all abandoned on the ground. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has stated that he intends to conduct investigations to plan for mining.

Since the arrival of the central army in the province, the communist bandits have been defeated and are now being pursued. It will not be difficult to eliminate them completely in the near future.

Xiamen Municipal Government Established: Inauguration Ceremony Held on the First. Siming County Government Simultaneously Abolished. Heshan Established as a Special District Office

Xiamen correspondence: The proposal to establish a municipality in Xiamen has been going on for nine years. The idea of establishing a municipality was conceived as early as when the Navy governed Xiamen in the 16th year of the Republic of China. Later, after several changes, it was never realized. After the 19th Route Army entered Fujian, the proposal to establish a municipality was re-raised, and a Siming City Preparatory Office was established, planning to abolish Siming County and establish Siming City on the entire island of Xiamen. Subsequently, the Executive Yuan ordered the Ministry of Interior, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Ministry of Navy to review the matter. As a result, the municipality was still limited to the scope of the Xiamen Public Security Bureau's police district, and the villages in Heshan outside the city still belonged to Siming County. This was because Xiamen was a commercial port with a mix of Chinese and foreigners, while Heshan belonged to the interior. Once it was included in the urban area, foreigners would use this as an excuse to break into the inland areas of Heshan. Moreover, Xiamen had a naval port command and fortress artillery, which were solid fortress defense areas. Therefore, the 19th Route Army used the director of the city preparatory office to concurrently serve as the county magistrate of Enming County to unify administration. This lasted throughout the period of the 19th Route Army, but the municipality was never established. During the puppet people's government era, a Xiamen municipal government was once established, but it was short-lived. After the Fujian Incident was quelled, the provincial government abolished the city preparatory office and established the Xiamen Special Public Security Bureau, which was a disguised municipal government in its rudimentary form, with Wang Gupan serving as the director and concurrently as the county magistrate of Siming. Later, the organization of the Special Public Security Bureau was reported to the Executive Yuan, but it was rejected by the Executive Yuan's meeting. Last winter, the provincial government again proposed the establishment of a municipality, which was submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. However, the area was still limited to the current police district. The Siming County Government was abolished, and Heshan was placed under the jurisdiction of Tong'an County. However, Xiamen Island is 30 li long and wide and 100 li in circumference, with a very large area. In addition to the city streets in the police district, which are several li long and wide, the rest originally belonged to the jurisdiction of the Siming County Government. The so-called Heshan is actually the entire island of Xiamen outside the police district. Tong'an County is separated by the sea, making jurisdiction inconvenient. Later, it was decided to change Heshan into a special district directly under the provincial government. On March 19th, the Executive Yuan approved Governor Chen Yi's request to appoint Wang Gupan as the mayor of Xiamen. Wang immediately went to the province to ask for instructions. The provincial government also ordered Wang to concurrently serve as the director of the Xiamen Public Security Bureau. Wang returned to Xiamen on the 29th, and the municipal government was established on April 1st.

The inauguration ceremony of the Xiamen Municipal Government was held at 10:00 AM on April 1st in the old Siming County Government. Foreign and Chinese guests were present, including consuls from Britain, the United States, Japan, and other countries stationed in Xiamen, Zhan Tiaoyuan and Chen Lianfen from the provincial party headquarters, Yao Juyuan and Wang Zhengmin from the county party headquarters, Naval Port Commander Lin Guogeng, Customs Superintendent Dai Ensai, and various institutions, chambers of commerce, and other organizations. First, Wang Gupan reported on the establishment process of the municipal government, followed by speeches by Zhan Tiaoyuan, Chen Lianfen, Lin Guogeng, and Hong Hongru, chairman of the chamber of commerce. Next, the Japanese consul and the British consul gave speeches. After the speeches, the ceremony was completed and the meeting adjourned. As for the Siming County Government, it was concluded and abolished on March 31st. The Heshan Special District Office was also established on the 1st. Wang Chengzhang, captain of the 2nd Marine Police Brigade, received an order from the provincial government to take over the county government and the county public security bureau, temporarily serving as the director of the district office. In addition to Wang Gupan concurrently serving as the director of the Public Security Bureau, the municipal government officials were announced on the same day: Yang Tingyu as the director of the Public Works Bureau, Shen Jing as the director of the Finance Bureau, Wang Zhengmin as the director of the 1st Section, Zheng Yongxiang as the director of the 2nd Section, and Ma Shaowen as the secretary. Also, Ma Shaowen concurrently serves as the chief of the general affairs section in the Public Security Bureau, Ye Bofu as the chief of the administrative section, Xu Chongyue as the chief of the judicial section, and Wang Zhaoduan as the chief of the health section. The organization of the municipal government is in accordance with the organizational outline approved by the provincial government. Originally, the municipal government was to have one bureau and three sections, namely the Public Security Bureau, the 1st Section (Finance), the 2nd Section (Public Utilities), and the 3rd Section (Social Affairs and Education). It was later changed to three bureaus and two sections, namely the Public Security Bureau, the Finance Bureau (formerly the 1st Section), the Public Works Bureau (formerly the 2nd Section), the 1st Section (Social Affairs), and the 2nd Section (Education), which were split from the original 3rd Section. (April 4th)

Wuxi: Dredging the Huangtian Port with Annual Earnings

The Jiangyin County Government has organized a dredging committee to be responsible for dredging the Huangtian Port waterway. The required cost is 160,000 yuan. In addition to the more than 60,000 yuan raised by the county, there is still a shortage of more than 90,000 yuan, which is impossible to raise. Therefore, Yan Puquan, the county magistrate of the county, and Wu Shuying, the chairman of the chamber of commerce, came to Wuxi together to borrow from the local silver merchants. The Wuxi Chamber of Commerce once invited representatives of various banks to discuss it at a meeting, but it did not produce results due to the extremely tight financial situation. However, the river is very important for the water conservancy and transportation of Xicheng, so at 10 o'clock yesterday (8th) morning, the Xiamen Chamber of Commerce invited representatives from nine banks, including China, Transportation, Jiangsu, Industry, Mainland, Xingye, Tongshang, Zhongnan, and Shanghai, to discuss it again. Representatives Wu Shuying, Gong Yinzeng, Han Xie'an, and Gu Haojia also came from Jiangyin. As a result of the discussion, it was decided that each bank would lend 4,000 yuan, totaling 36,000 yuan. In the future, the county will use the special construction funds from the province and county to repay it. The county will find a way to raise the remaining insufficient amount.

Eight-Year-Old Child Tragically Run Over and Killed by a Car

Ji Xuewen, a wheat purchasing agent at the Jiufeng Flour Mill, was marrying off his daughter yesterday (8th). The day before, the wedding dress was being tried on at the Railway Hotel, and his relative Tong Zizhen's family went to congratulate him. Tong Ziyansheng, only eight years old, happened to be playing at the entrance of the hotel when an unexpected tragedy occurred. Suddenly, a Rongtai car sped around the corner and knocked Ziyansheng down. The wheels ran over his head, crushing his skull. The patrol police immediately detained the driver Lin Fushou and sent him to the 6th Branch of the Public Security Bureau. They also sent the injured person to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, he was too badly injured and died shortly after. Afterwards, after repeated persuasion, the father of the deceased, Tong Zizhen, immediately put the body in a coffin and went to the county court to request an exemption from examination. He said that the dead cannot be brought back to life, so he would not make excessive demands. The driver Lin Fushou, who caused the accident, will be dealt with by the official authorities.

Robbery and Injury in Rural Areas

Cai Axing, a resident of Caijiaqiao in Dongqiao Town, 7th District, is a farmer and also sells bricks, tiles, and lime as a side business. His family of several people is barely able to make ends meet. Unexpectedly, at about 10:00 PM the night before, more than a dozen robbers suddenly came, each armed with pistols and other weapons. They first tied up the victim and burned his skin with fire, forcing him to reveal the location of his hidden silver. Then, they ransacked the chests and cabinets, looting at will. After about an hour, they escaped with their stolen goods, estimated at a loss of 170 to 180 yuan. Also, Gu Jinda, a villager in Daqiangmenkou Township, 8th District, was robbed the night before, with a loss of more than 300 yuan.

Changshu: Rice Industry Strike Resolved

The rice industry in this county experienced a strike because the Finance Department sent official Liu Xiang to Changshu to investigate accounts and increase business tax, which led to a conflict with Taifeng Rice Firm. A single misspoken word escalated into a full-scale strike, causing an immediate shortage of food. Prices in the Shanghai market soared, reaching over one yuan per stone. Rice milling operations here also ceased work, joining the turmoil. Subsequently, County Magistrate Zhai, along with Party Committee members Wu Zhongying and An Weinan, and Chamber of Commerce Chairman Pang Jiegong, personally went to the Rice Guild to persuade them. Finally, on the 7th, the entire industry temporarily resumed operations, bringing this turbulent event to a conclusion. As for the rice merchants' request to reduce taxes, the Chamber of Commerce and the Business Tax Bureau will explore alternative solutions.

Yangzhou: Yangzhou City Strike Calmed

A dispute arose between the Jiangdu Business Tax Bureau and the candle, charcoal, cloth, and incense industries due to account investigations, leading to the detention of shop employees. This sparked a reaction from 35 other industries. Although Commissioner Yan Shudong from the Provincial Department and members of the Chamber of Commerce intervened to mediate, a satisfactory resolution could not be reached. As a result, the detained employees of the Zhen Da, Baofeng, and Yufeng companies were not immediately released. Shop employees from various industries collectively called for rescue and petitioned the Party and government organs, but to no avail. Consequently, they declared a work slowdown. Capitalists also gathered to discuss providing strong support, and on the 7th, a unified general strike was declared to resist. Fearing this would affect social tranquility, the Party Headquarters and the County Government sent a letter requesting the County Chamber of Commerce to persuade the businesses to resume operations. A mediation meeting was held at the Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 PM on the 7th, attended by Commissioner Yan, County Magistrate Ma, Standing Committee members Yu and Zhang from the Party Headquarters' Executive and Supervisory Committee, Director Song of the Business Tax Bureau, all Executive and Supervisory Committee members of the Chamber of Commerce, and over 40 representatives from labor and management of various industries. County Magistrate Ma first expressed his views: (1) Those arrested would be released on bail, guaranteed by the County Party Headquarters; (2) All businesses must resume operations to prevent escalation; (3) They must abide by regulations and submit to account investigations, and if there are difficulties, they can request leniency. Subsequently, five resolutions were decided upon: (1) The County Government and Business Tax Bureau will jointly send personnel to assist with account investigations; (2) All businesses will resume operations starting from the 8th; (3) Omitted; (4) After the account investigations, local organizations will petition the Provincial Department for tax reductions; (5) In the future, shop employees shall not be arbitrarily arrested without cause. All attendees signed the above five resolutions. Representatives from various industries expressed satisfaction with the above resolutions. After the meeting, all labor representatives went to the County Government to welcome the arrested employees back to their stores.

Nantong: Xiang Zhizhuang's Inspection of Troops

The spring inspection of the security teams of various counties in the Nantong District will be held in Nantong. Xiang Zhizhuang, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Department, is scheduled to arrive in Nantong on the 9th. In addition to the graduating cadets of the second class of the district security team leader training course, the teams to be inspected this time include four platoons each from Nantong and Rugao, two platoons from Haimen, and one platoon each from Jingjiang, Qidong, and Chongming, as well as three platoons from the Industrial Security Team.

Hangzhou: Suicide of Vice President of the Red Swastika Society

Liu Daosheng, 73 years old, from Nanjing, Vice President and Vice Executive of the Southeast General Branch of the World Red Swastika Society, was recently assigned to Hangzhou to attend the Zhejiang Provincial Buddhist Association. He resided in room 81 of the Juying Hotel in the Xinshichang area. At 9:00 PM on the 7th, he took a rickshaw from the court to the lakeside, purchased lotus root flour and cigarettes, and asked the rickshaw puller to deliver them to the hotel. He then slowly walked to the Kaiyuan Bridge, where he suddenly suffered a nervous breakdown and jumped into the lake to commit suicide. Fortunately, a police officer heard the alarm, rescued him, and sent him to the relevant Public Security Bureau for questioning. He was ordered to return to the hotel to rest.

Audit Office Guardhouse Fire

At 10:30 AM on the 7th, a fire suddenly broke out in the guardhouse of the Liangzhe Salt Affairs Audit Office in Jin Yazhuang, Hangzhou, due to an electrical fault. Fire brigades and community fire rescue teams rushed to put out the blaze, which was eventually extinguished. An estimated three rooms of single-story buildings were burned down, with losses of approximately one thousand yuan. During the fire, several rows of guns and ammunition could not be evacuated in time and detonated, but fortunately, no one was injured.

Local News

Art Exhibition Preview Opens Yesterday - Over a Thousand Chinese and Western Visitors

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai preview of the London Exhibition of Chinese Art opened at 9:00 AM yesterday. Despite the severe weather, Chinese and Western visitors continued to arrive in succession. Among them, quite a few traveled from afar specifically to view and study various Chinese artworks. It is expected that when the weather improves today and tomorrow, even more visitors will attend. The situation yesterday is reported as follows:

Exhibits of Incalculable Value

Many of the antiques displayed at the exhibition are of incalculable value. Bronzes from the Shang and Zhou dynasties serve as ironclad evidence of China's earliest civilization. As for calligraphy and painting, they integrate works from various schools throughout history into one place, which should be effective for those studying this art form to achieve a thorough understanding. Moreover, various paintings, purely representative of Eastern flavor and not influenced by Western painting schools like modern Chinese paintings, will be even more impressive to people in London when exhibited there in the future. Furthermore, works such as Dong Beiyuan's "Dragon's Stay in Suburban Village" and Guo Xi's "Clearing Snow on Peaks" are all breathtaking. In particular, Emperor Qianlong's authentic works and Emperor Shizu's ink Zhong Kui are rarely seen outside, so attendees admire them endlessly.

Extracting the Essence to Glimpse the Whole Picture

Most of the antiques are selected from the Palace Museum and the Antiquities Exhibition Hall. In the past, when these antiques were displayed in the Palace Museum, each ticket cost one yuan, and it took three days to walk through all the palaces to see the whole picture. Now, extracting the essence and integrating the antiques sent by the Academia Sinica, the Peking Library, the Henan Museum, and the Anhui Provincial Library for exhibition, one can browse all of them in one day. This is much more economical in terms of both time and money.

Wang Shijie Summons Senior Personnel for Discussion

Yesterday morning, Minister of Education Wang Shijie visited the exhibition again and summoned senior personnel for discussion. The content concerned future preview arrangements and issues related to the shipment of antiques to England. Mr. Wang left the exhibition at 12:00 PM.

Adding Ticket Sales Points for More Convenience

Previously, to maintain order, the exhibition planned not to sell tickets at the entrance. Now, for the convenience of the audience, temporary ticket sales points have been set up at the entrance, as well as at various offices of the Bank of China and branches of the Shanghai Bank. Therefore, it will be more convenient for those who plan to visit in the future to purchase tickets.

Consulting Bilingual Catalogs

To facilitate the audience's participation in the explanation and browsing of antiques, the exhibition has specially printed detailed catalogs in both Chinese and English. The Chinese version costs five jiao (cents) of silver for printing costs, and the English version costs one yuan of silver. Both the appearance and content are very beautiful and substantial. In total, over a thousand copies of each language version were sold yesterday. The Commercial Press, which printed the books, is being urged to deliver them. People outside of Shanghai who wish to purchase the catalogs can also send payment to the exhibition.

Over Two Thousand Visitors Yesterday

Yesterday, over two thousand people visited the exhibition, half of whom were Chinese and foreign men and women. All had a high degree of appreciation for art, so they often discussed and elaborated on it. Foreigners especially praised calligraphy, painting, and kesi silk tapestries. The exhibition specifically displayed Chinese porcelain, famous worldwide, in a systematic manner starting from the Song Dynasty Ding Kiln, up to the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty. The progress of porcelain bodies, glazes, coloring, and patterns was particularly interesting.

Ye Gongchuo's Opinion on the Art Exhibition

Ye Gongchuo recently published his opinion on the "London International Exhibition of Chinese Art," which is worthy of reference for those who visit the exhibition. His opinion is transcribed as follows: "Our country's art and fine arts and crafts have always been world-renowned (except for a few people who lack understanding). However, our country has always lacked large-scale exhibition halls and specialized research institutions. Therefore, systematic collection, preservation, display, sorting, and circulation are all lacking. As a result, ordinary people who want to study our country's art often have no way to start and have to seek books written by foreigners and museums run by foreigners (although the Palace Museum and the Antiquities Exhibition Hall have many collections, their organization is not yet ready, so they cannot fully meet this need). Although our country's participation in the London International Exhibition of Our Country's Art this time may not achieve any major goals, it is enough to make ordinary people increase their understanding of our country's art or re-evaluate its value, so it is still a meaningful move. Opening a preview before going abroad to allow domestic people to have the opportunity to visit and study first is also a very appropriate method. There is a lot of discussion about the entire preparation process of this exhibition, but in all fairness, it is still an innovation for our country to handle such matters, so we cannot demand perfection. The most regrettable things seem to be two points: (1) Due to limitations on public products and various reasons, it is not possible to freely select them sufficiently. Therefore, there are doubts as to whether the products can represent the entirety of our country's art. (2) Due to various reasons, the products cannot be organized into a systematic and meaningful structure, which inevitably lacks the meaning of 'history.' Therefore, it is sufficient for appreciation but slightly lacks the function of research. The causes of these two are also very complicated, so I will not elaborate on them for now. I only hope that the authorities will solicit the opinions of experts more when handling such matters in the future before proceeding. It is also necessary to prepare sufficient time and not hand in the papers in a hurry at the last minute. If exhibiting abroad, it is even more necessary to know oneself and the enemy, and carefully determine the plan and steps, so as to avoid improper responses and wasting financial resources. That's all. As for this exhibition, it can generally be divided into six categories: calligraphy and painting, porcelain, bronze, silk embroidery, lacquerware, and jade. The total number of calligraphy and painting is 163 pieces. The Palace Museum accounts for eight tenths of the products. The rest are the products of the Antiquities Exhibition Hall. In my personal opinion, I wish to fully select and send representative calligraphy and paintings from various schools throughout history to show the truth about our country's calligraphy and painting schools. However, in fact, the calligraphy and paintings of these two institutions are not complete in all schools (there are also some that are not good). The standards for selection by each person cannot be completely consistent. There are also other facts that must be bound. Therefore, the result is like the currently selected catalog. This catalog has been approved by Chinese and British experts and reviewed by the preparatory committee. Although I dare not say that all the fine products of our country's calligraphy and painting are prepared here, it can be asserted that there is no inferior thing in this catalog. As for the works of each family, there are some that cannot represent the achievements of their lives, such as Mi Nan Gong and Zhao Ziang's paintings, which are not their most exquisite works. This is limited by the facts and there is nothing that can be done about it (the Palace Museum lost a lot of collections one after another before the Qing Dynasty. After the Republic of China, even more were lost before Puyi left the palace. Even Puyi's list of rewards alone included more than 1,800 pieces of calligraphy and painting, all of which were the essence of the Six Dynasties, Tang, Song, Yuan, and Ming dynasties). However, famous dramatic works such as Dong Beiyuan's "Dragon's Stay in Suburban Village" and Guo Xi's "Clearing Snow on Peaks" are all breathtaking and sufficient to overwhelm everything. The Qing Palace's collection of porcelain is more complete than other items. This time, after Mr. Guo Baochang carefully selected them in Beijing and re-examined them in Shanghai, the products are excellent, and the styles of various kilns of all dynasties are roughly complete. It is estimated that domestic and foreign collections will never be so complete. It is a pity that the pottery and porcelain before the Song Dynasty were not collected. This is also due to the limitations of the Palace Museum. There are not many bronzes exhibited this time. Judging from the quality and quantity of the various utensils unearthed recently, this product is not enough to represent them. However, our country's research on bronzes has always emphasized writing, followed by style and patterns. In terms of writing, this type of product is also very impressive. In addition, silk embroideries include various Song Dynasty kesi silk tapestries, including landscapes, figures, flowers, and birds. They are truly spectacular (this type of kesi silk is rarely seen in the South). The kesi silk of the Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties is also a fine product. Kesi silk embroidery was originally unique to the South, but it has now declined and been lost. It is a pity (there are still people in Mudu, Suzhou who can make kesi silk, and embroidery workers in Jiangsu, Hunan, and Guangdong are famous, but in fact, they are far inferior to the past). As for carved lacquerware, there are Yongle, Xuande, Jiajing, and Qianlong of the Ming Dynasty and Qianlong of the Qing Dynasty. Jade articles are mostly better in workmanship. If you want to study our country's ancient jade, you cannot rely on the Palace Museum's collections as data. Most Chinese people know this, so there is no need to repeat it. This London exhibition seeks Chinese artworks collected by various countries, not specifically from our country. Many of our country's artworks have flowed abroad over the years, and what we have may not be as good as others. If we intend to compete, we must actively organize in advance. However, the organizations of our country's public and private institutions are mostly unsound, and it is very difficult for them to gather and act. After this time, the Chinese people will increase their awareness and experience, and there will be good hopes in the future. Furthermore, in recent times, those who reject spiritual civilization often say that what is needed today is material construction. Anything else is not urgent. They do not take the preservation of antiques seriously. They do not know that the national spirit of a country is often tied to past cultural relics. Therefore, from Soviet Russia on the left to Italy on the right, all arts and fine arts are extremely promoted and protected. However, their purpose is different from our country's past practice of only providing for personal enjoyment. Therefore, our country should quickly build mass art, preserve and promote inherent art as the foundation, and not only provide for personal enjoyment or blindly destroy things. This is also what I hope from the audience of the preview, who will be inspired by the wind."

English Name Slightly Changed

The advertisement published by the exhibition in the English-language North-China Daily News and the China Press was originally The Preliminary Exhibition of The London Exhibition of Chinese Art. The four committee members specially sent to China by the United Kingdom believed that the scope was too broad and requested that it be changed to ... of Chinese National Treasures Selected for The International Exhibibition of Chinese in London 1935-36. The exhibition has agreed and instructed the above two newspapers to correct it today.

An Expert Talks About the Selection Process

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency met with an expert who participated in the selection yesterday morning. According to the discussion, many of the items on display this time are very precious. Among them, Shang and Zhou bronzes are treasures in our country's history and are unparalleled among the world's antiques. Porcelain from famous kilns of the Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties is also a special product of our country. Because porcelain is inconvenient to carry, less of it has flowed abroad. This exhibition in England is still an innovation. Ancient books are the world's earliest printed books and are especially valuable. The Peking Library originally did not allow ancient books to participate. After repeated requests from the preparatory committee, they finally agreed to transport them here. As for ancient calligraphy and paintings, because many have flowed out, foreigners have a good ability to identify them. The five experts sent by the United Kingdom were extremely strict in selecting them. They used microscopes to examine all paintings on silk. A British expert recognized a pot shape in a certain ancient painting from the Southern Song Dynasty as a Qing object and suspected that it was not genuine, so it was rejected. However, foreigners are superstitious about emperors and only selected those with Emperor Qianlong and Jiaqing's imperial seals, which led to the failure of some famous paintings to be selected. As for the works of Lang Shining, the preparatory committee believed that Lang was a Westerner and could not represent our country's culture, so they planned not to select them. Later, at the request of the British Committee, two paintings were selected. As for the jade articles, they were relatively inferior.

Zhang Fakui Visits This Newspaper Yesterday, Hosted by Ma Yinliang

Former Commander of the Fourth Army, Mr. Zhang Fakui, has been traveling around Europe and the United States, investigating various political, economic, military, and social aspects for nearly three years. After returning to China on the 12th of last month, he made a brief stay in Shanghai and is quite concerned about various social undertakings. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Mr. Zhang, accompanied by Chen Jitang's representatives Yang Dezhao, Chen Zhuohong, Zhu Buyun, and other gentlemen, came to visit this newspaper. They were hosted by the manager of this newspaper, Ma Yinliang, who accompanied them to visit various departments such as business, distribution, editing, and printing machinery. Mr. Zhang inquired in detail about the history and distribution of this newspaper. Mr. Zhang believes that the number of newspaper readers in our country is not universal compared to European and American countries, and hopes that the people of the country will work hard to promote education so that all the people in the country can have the possibility of holding a newspaper in their hands, and then the country can be strong.
