Aviator Sun Tonggang Sails to Italy Tomorrow, Various Circles Host Farewell Banquet Yesterday Afternoon

Youthful aviator Sun Tonggang, who flew a monoplane back to his motherland from Germany last year, was warmly welcomed by people across the country. Recently, in order to seek further study, he plans to go to Italy to continue studying aeronautical engineering. This time, he went to Jinjing via Jinan to complete the formalities for going abroad, which has already been completed. He arrived in Shanghai by the Beijing-Shanghai train the day before yesterday and stayed at the New Asia Hotel.

Public Farewell Banquet from Various Circles

The various circles of this city and all members of the Heng Society specially hosted a farewell banquet at the Atlantic Hotel yesterday afternoon. Over 200 people attended, including Du Yuesheng, Jin Tingsun, Yuan Ludeng, Wang Yansong, Yu Qiaqing, Lu Jingshi, and Zhu Xuefan. The banquet was chaired by Du Yuesheng. During the banquet, Zhu Xuefan delivered a speech on behalf of the attendees, stating that Mr. Sun is a promising talent in our country's aviation industry. This trip to Italy for study will surely enable him to serve the country when he returns after completing his studies. Next, guest Wang Yansong gave a speech, stating that Mr. Sun is going to Italy to investigate and introduce the spirit of foreign science to the country, and will surely make great contributions in the future. Mr. Yuesheng has been sparing no effort in promoting aviation and has especially supported Comrade Sun. In the future, it is hoped that Comrade Sun will continue to work hard together with the spirit promoted by Mr. Yuesheng, and the future is boundless. Next, Yuan Ludeng gave a speech, stating that in the past, traffic was inconvenient, so the evolution of the country was slow. Since the invention of the airplane, there has been an amazing development in transportation. Foreign science is developed, so progress is very fast, while our country is lagging behind. This is all caused by the lack of good talents. Mr. Sun is a good talent among young people. It is hoped that Mr. Sun will have good results after the investigation and contribute to the country. Next, Du Yuesheng gave a speech, stating that Comrade Sun's first step has been successful. This trip abroad is the second time. It is hoped that his success will be greater than the first time, so as not to disappoint those who are enthusiastic about promoting aviation. Finally, Mr. Sun gave a speech to thank everyone, and the event ended with a group photo.

Sailing Abroad Tomorrow

According to Mr. Sun yesterday, in addition to investigating aviation, he will also study the latest inventions in various scientific technologies in order to seek further study. It has now been scheduled for the 10th (ie, tomorrow - at 12 noon, he will embark on the Italian mail ship "Lotovandis"). The trip will last one year.

Wang Shijie, Zeng Zhongming, Fu Rulin, Chu Minyi, Liu Weichi, Ye Rongcang, Liu Ruiheng, Zou Lin, etc., took the night express to Jinjing yesterday.

Envoy He to Depart Tomorrow for Post

Last night's farewell reception for the press, according to the Central News Agency, stated that Mr. He Yaozu, the appointed envoy to Turkey, is scheduled to depart tomorrow on the Italian mail steamer "Conte Verde" for Europe and then Turkey to take up his new post. Last night at 7 PM, at the New Asia Restaurant, he hosted a reception for the local press, attended by over fifty reporters from various newspapers and news agencies. During the dinner, Mr. He elaborated on his aspirations as an envoy in great detail. After his speech, Yan Duhe responded on behalf of the press and raised a toast to the envoy's health. The gathering adjourned around 9 PM. Mr. He's speech is recorded below: Today, I am very pleased to have this opportunity to gather with all of you. I feel I have much to say, but because I am not good at public speaking, I fear I will not be able to fully express myself. In any democratic country, public opinion is respected. Therefore, the term "public opinion" is not only receiving increasing attention from Europeans and Americans, but also from our own people more than before. As the Book of Documents says, "Heaven sees as my people see; Heaven hears as my people hear." This shows that ancient politics also valued public opinion. But further, how is public opinion expressed? Public discourse is an expression of public opinion, or at least a part of it. How is public discourse created? Who leads the people? Considering the saying, "Those who know first enlighten those who know later; those who are awakened first awaken those who are awakened later," those who create public discourse and lead the people are, of course, people with excellent knowledge and status in society. In my view, leaders in the press, due to their position and opportunities, have the greatest power to lead the people and shape public opinion. This view is not entirely based on idealism, but rather a conclusion drawn from observing the facts. For example, in the past, many unfortunate events occurred. The domestic press either adopted a passive attitude or published active commentary. The resolution of the Fujian Incident, for example, was significantly influenced by the press. This is a well-known fact and need not be elaborated. In short, the various improvements in Chinese society over the past few decades owe much to the help of public discourse. The success of any improvement is either due to the advocacy of the press beforehand, or the support of the press afterwards, enabling it to achieve twice the result with half the effort, easily. Otherwise, one will inevitably get half the result with twice the effort, and achieve little with great labor. Furthermore, the power of public discourse is not only related to the reform of domestic affairs, but also to the success or failure of diplomacy. This is true not only in China, but also in other advanced countries. At this point, I not only want to express my sincere respect to everyone present, but also to convey my ardent expectations to the entire press. For the sake of searching for ways to improve our country's economy and the people's livelihood, and for the sake of spreading the gospel of world peace and international cooperation, I wish you all good health and urge you to work hard. This time I, Yaozu, am going to Turkey as an envoy for the first time. I have no experience in diplomacy. Turkey has not yet established an embassy in our country, and our country's establishment of an embassy in Turkey is also a new venture. I am shallow in learning and dare not say that I can be competent for such an important mission. I can only do my best, with the interests of the country as the premise and the opinions of the people as the backing. I will consider matters carefully in order to live up to my mission. Since the government announced my appointment as envoy to Turkey, many public and private organizations and public discourse institutions have generously offered advice, either providing instructions on Sino-Turkish diplomacy, or inquiring about the causes and effects of Turkey's rejuvenation. This is a symbol of the general public's attention to national affairs. I feel an extraordinary sense of joy in my heart, and I feel I have much to say. However, before I reach my destination and conduct on-the-ground research, I dare not express too many opinions. Moreover, on today's occasion, I am limited by time and cannot express too many opinions. But I very much hope to provide relevant domestic agencies and organizations with actual research data on Turkey, or the results of my research, whenever possible, for reference. Regarding the facts of Turkey's rejuvenation and the comparison of national politics between China and Turkey, I gave a report at the Central Party Headquarters the other day. Although this report has been disclosed in a few newspapers, I am afraid that some of my compatriots are still unaware of it. Therefore, I would like to give a brief statement of the main points of the report the other day. First, let's talk about the comparison of nationalities: (1) Both nationalities are yellow. Furthermore, because nearly 100,000 Turks surrendered to our country during the fourth year of the Zhenguan reign of Emperor Taizong of Tang, and lived in China, it has been more than 1,300 years now. Turks can intermarry with Han and Hui people. Therefore, the bloodlines of the two races should be somewhat similar. (2) However, due to differences in location and climate, the Turkish people were still nomadic in the Middle Ages and early modern times. Our country has long been engaged in agriculture. Before the Zhou Dynasty, it had already become a farming nation. (3) The Turkish people's lives were still very simple hundreds of years ago, and their residences were not fixed. Therefore, there were frequent migrations. Our people's lives are complex and comfortable, so they have always been attached to their homeland. (4) In the past, the Turkish people had a very strong sense of self and did not easily accept foreign cultures and ideas. Our people have always been inclusive and have the power of assimilation. They are quite capable of embracing foreign cultures. (5) The Turkish people have never been completely conquered by other races. Therefore, they are stubborn and upright, with a spirit of adventure and enterprise. Unfortunately, the Han people were once conquered by the Yuan and Qing dynasties, which inevitably reduced the nation's self-esteem and self-confidence. As a result, our people lack a sense of national consciousness and political interest, and ambitious

Envoy He Yaozu to Turkey (in the center, standing) (Photo by Qichang)

Page 10

countries have harbored thoughts of coveting and invading Russia. Now let's talk about the political comparison: (1) Both countries are large countries in Asia, but our country is larger, richer in resources, more populous, has a longer history, and a more complex social organization than Turkey (the area of ​​the territory is one to ten, and the number of people is about one to thirty). (2) The political systems of both countries were first monarchical autocracy and then democratic republic, but the time of our country's monarchical system and democratic system is longer (Turkey's democratic country was established in the twelfth year of the Republic of China). (3) Both countries have repeatedly expanded their territory and promoted their national prestige, but the strategies adopted are quite different. Turkey completely adopts the method of conquest (such as conquering various Balkan ethnic groups), which is close to hegemonic rule. Our country has always advocated the politics of benevolent rule, such as "If the San Miao do not submit, then dance with axes and shields, and the San Miao will come to submit themselves." The spirit of benevolent rule has enabled the Xianbei, Khitan, Jurchen, Miao, and Man ethnic groups to assimilate in history, and it is often used to integrate small ethnic groups nearby (for example, the policy of appeasement towards Korea, Vietnam, Burma, Siam, etc.). (4) In the past hundred years, both countries have experienced many internal conflicts, but the reasons and nature of the internal conflicts are different. In the 19th century, the foreign races ruled in the Turkish Empire were stimulated by the revolutionary ideology and often caused internal chaos and became independent. The alien races ruled in our country rarely rebelled and became independent. After the establishment of the Turkish democratic country, the nation was very united. Even the two revolutions before its establishment adopted peaceful means to avoid bloodshed. People of the same race in our country often engage in internal strife, and even after the establishment of the Republic of China, there have been several meaningless wars. This may be because the number of Han people is dozens of times more than that of the Turkish people, and our people are confined to the evolution of history and cannot change their mistakes and move towards good. (5) In the past hundred years, both have suffered from foreign aggression, have been bullied by great powers and exploited economically, and have lost many territories, lost part of their national sovereignty, and signed various unequal treaties (the most obvious are the consular jurisdiction and tariff restriction clauses). Now Turkey has restored its national sovereignty and achieved its goals. Our country should learn from the worthy, and give our whips a fierce crack, a few points that can be compared have been briefly described, and now I will put forward the factors that I personally believe are the key to Turkey's successful revival, and the characteristics that our country can learn from, and ask you for advice. (1) The most surprising thing about studying Turkey's revival is why Turkey was able to turn danger into safety in a year or so after the European War, when it was surrounded by enemies and at the end of its rope. In order to find this answer, we discovered the biggest difference between Turkey and our country, that is, when the Turkish people are in turmoil, they are sincerely, absolutely, and harmoniously united. They never have civil wars, and they always concentrate and unanimously face the outside world. This is the first factor in their success in the shortest possible time. (2) Although the Turkish people's lack of infighting is a successful factor, it is only a positive advantage. If we explore its positive factors, it is of course because there is a wise leader who awakens and organizes the people of the whole country, especially because the majority of the people can deeply understand the country's difficulties and uniformly obey disciplined leadership and work hard to move forward. Otherwise, whether it can break through the serious national crisis is still a big question. In other words, a wise leader, a good organization, strict discipline, an enterprising and united people are the second factor for Turkey's revival in the shortest possible time. (3) What is also worthy of special attention is the Turkish National Army. Everyone knows that Asia Minor is the place where the Turkish people live. It is for the survival of the Turkish people and the survival of the Turkish people. They do not care about any sacrifices. Therefore, the Greek army will not withdraw from Asia Minor for a day, and the National Army will continue to attack for a day. This kind of army organized for the purpose of protecting the survival of its country, this kind of spirit of identifying the enemy, vowing to fight to the death, and adhering to fearlessness is not only the central force for the revival of Turkey, but also the soul of the revival of the Turkish nation. This is the third factor in their success in the shortest possible time. (4) Finally, to make a further exploration, when Turkey was surrounded by enemies, the enemies of the National Army were very numerous. In addition to the Greeks, there were also British and French armies. Although the Turkish National Army was brave, it was outnumbered and the situation was very critical. In 1921, the French and Italian armies withdrew their troops, and the situation changed. Why did the two countries suddenly withdraw their troops? Was it because they were afraid of the fighting power of the Turkish National Army? Absolutely not. The reason why the governments of France and Italy ordered the withdrawal of troops was because the Turkish National Government had a real and tacit understanding with the two countries and concluded a mutually beneficial agreement. If the Turkish Nationalist Party cannot distinguish the priorities and take a broad view, it will not be able to identify the main enemy. If it does not have a complete diplomatic policy, it will not be willing to use lures to lure the enemy, nor will it be able to make the invaders disrupt their own lines. Therefore, sensitive diplomacy and diplomacy with foresight are the fourth factor for them to complete the revival in the shortest possible time. Not long ago, the great powers regarded Turkey as a sick man, and it was not enough to bully him and exploit him. They tried every means to seize his property. After the European War, Turkey was in a more dangerous position than our country today. But after several years of struggle and effort, the atmosphere has been renewed. He is competing with the great powers on the international political stage, and the great powers have to look at him differently. Our country is vast in territory, rich in resources, and has a large population. If the whole country can be uplifted and united, and the factors of Turkey's successful revival can be used as a lesson, and everything is implemented in a practical way, wouldn't it be possible to compete with the great powers at a rate of thousands of miles a day, not just keep pace with Turkey? Thank you very much for your presence tonight. In two days, I will be leaving the country. I would like to take this opportunity to say goodbye to everyone. Before parting, I would like to say one more thing: whether before or after I leave, no matter who has any advice, I will sincerely welcome it. Finally, please join me in a toast, wishing the Republic of China long live, and wishing the Chinese people peace and happiness.

4,160,000 British Silver Dollars: Three Banks Withdrew from the Treasury Yesterday; China Bank Assigned Personnel to be Responsible for Loading and Unloading

The silver dollars ordered by the Central, China, and Communications Banks from London, England, in addition to the first batch of 3,000,000 that had already been shipped to Shanghai, the second and third batches were also shipped to Shanghai on the "Radnorshire" of the British company the other day. They were unloaded and stored in the treasury by the three banks yesterday morning. Yesterday, the reporter from the Industrial and Commercial News Agency visited Mr. Zhao Yuanding of the Customs Section of the Documentation Department and Mr. Wu Ziliang of the Cash Department of the Bank of China to inquire about the exact amount of the second and third batches of British silver dollars. According to them, the British side initially telegraphed the three banks that the amount of silver was originally 2,925,000 yuan, which was loaded on the "Radnorshire," and 1,000,000 yuan was loaded on the "Nardana." Later, due to the lack of silver on the British side, only 2,925,000 yuan was loaded on the "Radnorshire," and Hong Kong was telegraphed to add 1,235,000 yuan, totaling 4,160,000 yuan, which was loaded on the "Radnorshire" to Shanghai. The distribution method is 1,664,000 yuan for the Central Bank, 1,664,000 yuan for the Bank of China, and 832,000 yuan for the Communications Bank. At about 7:00 this morning (i.e., yesterday morning), I (Mr. Zhao referred to himself) was responsible for supervising the coolies to unload the goods at the Hongkou Gonghexiang Wharf. The work was not completed until 3:00 in the afternoon. The silver was distributed according to the distribution and transported to the three banks for storage and use, they said.

Shanghai: Anti-Epidemic Meeting Held Yesterday; Director of the National Health Administration, Liu Ruiheng, Came to Shanghai to Participate; Seven Measures for Preventing Cholera Were Agreed Upon

Every summer is the time when cholera is most likely to spread, and it is highly infectious and harmful. Thanks to the efforts of prevention over the years, the harm has been greatly reduced in this city, and it has not occurred in the past two years. This year, because it is already late spring and early summer, various health agencies are again paying attention to the prevention of cholera. Yesterday, a meeting was held at the Municipal Government to discuss the implementation of the joint prevention of cholera in Shanghai this year. It was presided over by Liu Ruiheng, Director of the National Health Administration. Attendees included Jin Baoshan, Deputy Director of the Central Health Laboratory, Wu Liande, Director of the Seaport Quarantine Office, Wu Changyao, Section Chief, Li Tingan, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, Chen Zongxian, Director of the Central Epidemic Prevention Office, Huang Zifang, Section Chief of the Health Section of the Two-Road Administration Bureau, Cheng Shuzhen, Director of the Health Laboratory, Wang Shiwei, Technical Specialist of the Municipal Health Bureau, Lan Ansheng, Health Expert, Deng Sigen, Pathologist, Jordan, Director of the Public Concession Health Department, Lai Baode, Director of the French Concession Health Bureau, and Xie Jieyang, a doctor from the hospital. It was decided that: (1) All implementation work will continue to be carried out according to the established practice of last year. (2) Cheng Muyi and Yang Yongnian will be added to the anti-epidemic group committee. (3) Alan will be added to the propaganda group. (4) Anti-epidemic work will be implemented from May 1st. (5) The amount of cholera vaccine injections will remain the same. (6) 300 bottles of vaccine manufactured by the Municipal Health Laboratory, each cubic centimeter containing 400 million bacteria, will be used for trial use in the Health Bureau. (7) The proposals of the epidemic prevention institute will be submitted to the anti-epidemic group for review. It was also agreed that any new ideas on epidemic prevention will be submitted for discussion after the end of the annual prevention work.

Japanese Merchants' Activities in China: Organize an Inspection Team to Tour the Yangtze River; Repairing the Yunyang Maru to Resume Navigation to Yichang and Chongqing

Japanese merchants are now actively restoring trade with China. Japanese ships that have been suspended for more than three years are also planned to resume service one after another. The following is a report on the recent activities of the large-scale Japanese commercial inspection team and the Nisshin Shipping's resuming service on the Yangtze River.

Inspection Team Comes to China: Japan is singing high praises for friendship with China. Therefore, the major Japanese commercial firms and manufacturing plants in Osaka have specially organized a Chinese inspection team, including hardware, machinery, metal products, stationery, electrical materials, automobiles, fountain pens, drawing materials, pump engines, mining, phonographs, waterproof equipment, groceries, oil paper, and other merchants, such as Shibazaki, Hirakichi, Chogen, Marutaka, Yoshinosuke Sakai, Ito, Funaoka, Nishimura, Kyokichi, Imai Suzuki, Yoshikin, Hasegawa, etc., a total of 26 manufacturers and dealers, in order to develop trade with China and promote Japanese goods, will conduct detailed inspections in southern China and the Yangtze River basin, in order to restore the situation before January 28th. They have already departed from Osaka and arrived in Shanghai on the Nagasaki Maru. They will only stay in Shanghai for one day and will take the Shanghai-Nanjing train to the capital yesterday. After inspecting in Nanjing, they will go to various places along the Yangtze River. This trip will last for one month and aims to inspect what kind of goods China needs, and then promote the sales of Japanese goods in China.

Yunyang Maru Resumes Navigation: The Nisshin Shipping Company's Yangtze River ships originally had 25 ships. After January 28th, only four ships were operating, and the rest were suspended. Last year, one ship was opened between Hankou and Yichang. Recently, another Yueyang Maru has been added to the Yangtze River in the past week. A total of six ships are operating. Recently, because Japanese goods are expected to be sold in China, the Tokyo headquarters of the Nisshin Shipping Company has decided to resume service one after another on the ships that have been suspended, taking a gradual approach. Therefore, the company has repaired the Yunyang Maru, which has been abandoned in Shanghai for more than three years, and began to send it to Yichang and Chongqing yesterday.

Bureau of Social Affairs Promotes the Establishment of Worker-Farmer Cooperatives

Since the Bureau of Social Affairs has actively promoted cooperative enterprises in this city, a vigorous atmosphere has emerged. The general public has also gradually understood the meaning of cooperatives, and there is no shortage of people who can organize them on their own initiative. Therefore, the number of cooperatives is also increasing day by day. The Bureau’s recent progress and plans for promoting cooperative enterprises are detailed below:

(1) Promoting Workers' Consumer Cooperative Enterprises

Motivation for Promotion

This city is a major industrial center in the country. According to recent statistics, there are more than 360,000 factory workers (and about 300,000 dock and transportation workers). These workers rely mainly on wages. However, because there is no organization of consumer cooperatives, the purchase of daily necessities is subject to layer upon layer of exploitation by middlemen, and workers' livelihoods are invisibly reduced. As a result, they are in a state of poverty and distress and cannot extricate themselves, even leading to major problems such as unemployment, which disrupt the order of social peace. Therefore, the promotion of workers' consumer cooperatives is an urgent matter that cannot be delayed. This is not only sufficient to solve the economic oppression suffered by ordinary workers, but also indirectly maintain social peace. The implementation plan is recorded below:

Zoning

The organization of workers' consumer cooperatives in this city is based on the zoning of workers in this city. The first district includes the Southern District; the second district includes the French Concession; the third district includes the Public Concession, west of North Sichuan Road and south of Suzhou Creek; the fourth district includes the Public Concession, east of North Sichuan Road; the fifth district includes the four districts of Yangjing Pond Bridge, Luxing, and Yangsi; the sixth district includes the two districts of Zhabei and Pengpu; the seventh district includes the three districts of Jiangwan, Yinxiang, and Yinhang; the eighth district includes the three districts of Wusong and Gaoqiao; the ninth district includes the two districts of Fahua and Caojing; the tenth district includes the Pusong District; and the eleventh district includes the Zhenru District. All factories that usually employ more than 300 workers should establish a worker consumer cooperative in each factory. Factories with fewer workers should jointly establish a cooperative with two or more factories nearby. However, small-scale factories that believe it is necessary to establish a consumer cooperative and are willing to voluntarily organize it may do so at their convenience. Consumer Cooperatives.

Phased Implementation

The area of this city is vast, and if it is held at the same time, there will be many difficulties in carrying out the work. It will be held in three phases, step by step, to achieve the effect of universalization. The first phase is the first district, the second phase is the second, third, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts, and the third phase is the seventh, eighth, ninth, tenth, and eleventh districts. The name of the consumer cooperative should be a certain factory (company or society). After the consumer cooperatives in the factories in the first phase have achieved results, the second and third phases of the districts listed above will be held. However, factories in each district that are willing to organize consumer cooperatives on their own initiative may do so at their convenience. After most of the factories in each district have established consumer cooperatives, they should immediately begin to organize the joint consumer cooperative of each district. When starting to organize the joint cooperative, the members of the trade union in each district should be responsible for preparing it, and they may borrow the trade union address as the office of the joint cooperative.

Publicity and Guidance

In terms of publicity, it is divided into (1) printing small booklets to explain the essence of consumer cooperation, organizational methods, and a summary of operations in popular language, and distributing them to trade unions and factories in various districts; (2) organizing cooperation lectures, with the Bureau hiring people with knowledge and experience in cooperation to give regular lectures on the principles of consumption, organization, and operational methods, etc., and ordering those in charge of the trade unions in each district to come to the Bureau to listen to the lectures, and then the trade unions in each district will be responsible for publicizing them to the factories. In addition, lecture meetings may tour various districts as needed by the environment; (3) trade unions and factories in each district, except for those that have labor schools or lecture meetings, etc., which are specifically for workers to receive supplementary education, should try their best to explain the principles and operations of cooperatives to workers, so that even illiterate workers can have a considerable understanding. Regarding guidance, if the operations of the consumer cooperatives or joint cooperatives of factories in various districts of this city are not very appropriate or there are errors in handling them when they are newly established, the Bureau should send personnel to assess and guide them at any time; (1) the Bureau should select personnel with rich cooperative knowledge and experience and assign them as instructors to assess and guide the consumer cooperatives or joint cooperatives of factories in various districts at any time; (2) if the consumer cooperatives or joint cooperatives in each district believe that detailed guidance is necessary, they may send personnel to reside in each district temporarily to provide roving guidance; (3) when the factory inspectors of the Bureau go to various factories to inspect, they should pay attention to and guide the consumer cooperatives that have been established at any time.

Carrying out Screening

(1) When the consumer cooperatives or joint cooperatives of factories in each district are first established, they should register with the Bureau in accordance with the procedures; (2) after screening the consumer cooperatives or joint cooperatives established by factories in each district, the Bureau will approve those that are considered to have achieved results for registration; (3) consumer cooperatives or joint cooperatives of factories in each district that are deemed to have achieved excellent results after screening may be given the following rewards by the Bureau: A, issuing a commendation order; B, awarding medals or certificates of merit; (4) consumer cooperatives or joint cooperatives of factories in each district that are deemed to be poorly managed after screening may be given the following punishments: A, issuing an order of censure; B, those who still fail to improve after being censured in writing more than twice may be ordered to reorganize. After the plan has been submitted by the Bureau to the Municipal Government for approval, six factory consumer cooperative instructors will be recruited to take charge of the investigation, publicity, and guidance work. The South Shanghai District has now been designated to conduct a pilot project, and instructors are sent to various factories on a daily basis to provide guidance and help them organize consumer cooperatives. At present, 13 cooperatives have been established in various factories in this city, and about 20 are in preparation (to be continued).

The Shanghai Municipal Council Resolves to Ban Small Taxis Small Cars May Be in Danger after One Year of Operation

The Shanghai Taxi Association petitioned the Shanghai Municipal Council to run small cars, charging six cents for each delivery or twenty minutes. This proposal was carefully considered by the Transportation Committee and investigated in Singapore, Penang, Manila, and other places. According to the opinion of the Commissioner of Police, the existing taxis are sufficient for use, and the price is not expensive. The number of cars has not increased or decreased much in the past six years, and there is no need to limit it for the time being. It is difficult to say what the impact will be if small cars are allowed to run. However, he believes that the current taxis are most suitable for the current situation, and Shanghai cannot be compared with other ports. It is impossible to set up parking spaces for this type of vehicle, and small cars are damaged very quickly, so they must be inspected every month. Moreover, cars soliciting customers along the road have almost replaced rickshaws in Tokyo and Kobe, Japan, but this has increased a difficult problem for the police. After detailed discussion by the committee, it was considered that small cars could be tried, but with the following conditions: (1) No parking or soliciting customers on the street is allowed; (2) Passengers are limited to three people in addition to the driver; (3) The vehicle's manufacturing style must be approved by the Commissioner of Police and must pass the inspection on time. After this proposal was submitted to the board of directors meeting, the Commissioner of Police stated his opinion, saying that the structure of small cars is originally not durable and may be dangerous after one year of operation, and frequent inspections will also increase the expenses of the Shanghai Municipal Council. Moreover, the operating cost of small cars is no less than that of large cars, and it may not be beneficial to the car line. If the business of large cars is defeated, the small car style cannot be supported. Then, after discussion by the directors, the majority agreed with the Commissioner of Police's opinion and decided that, for the sake of transportation benefits, it would not be convenient to approve the application for small taxi operating licenses. It is found that the weight of the current taxis is about 2,250 pounds to 3,000 pounds, and the license fee for the concession is 33 yuan to 36 yuan per quarter. As for the so-called small car, the weight is about 1,000 to 1,500 pounds, and the license fee per quarter should be 27 yuan.

Lin Shaofang Embezzles 50,000 Yuan from His Father The Police Report No Arrest and Issue an Arrest Warrant Shaofang Recently Returned to Shanghai and Was Detained Awaiting Trial

Lin Yiquan, the owner of Lin's Garden at No. 110 North Sichuan Road, is a Cantonese with a solid family fortune. His second son, Lin Shaofang, graduated from Soochow University. In the autumn of the 18th year of the Republic of China, he was introduced to work at the Shanghai Hong Kong National Bank at No. 348 Jiangxi Road. From August to October, his father successively gave him 50,000 yuan to deposit in the bank to earn interest. However, he secretly used the above silver dollars as speculative gold trading capital and lost it all. He used a fake receipt to prevaricate his father. At the end of the year, Lin Yiquan went to the bank to check the deposit and found that it had all been embezzled by his son. Shaofang took the opportunity to escape to Fengtian at 6 pm on December 31. His father, together with the bank, reported to the police for arrest but to no avail. On January 4 of the following year, he issued an arrest warrant to the First Special District Court. On January 11 of the 20th year of the Republic of China, he hired lawyer Huang Yuping to publish an arrest warrant with a reward of 1,000 yuan, but no trace could be found. His father could only sigh in vain and had no way to do anything. Shaofang was short of money and drifted in a foreign land, which was not the end of the story. After thinking again and again, there was no better solution, so he returned to Shanghai to inquire about the news. He stayed in a certain hotel. At 4:45 pm the day before yesterday, he was passing by the vicinity of Bazilu North Jiangxi Road when he was caught by his fellow villager and relative Pan Jianqing. He refused to go home and quarreled with each other. The Nanjing Road Citizens' Association Releases Telephone Usage Statistics Obtained from a Survey of Shops on Nanjing Road

The Shanghai Telephone Company has increased its prices again this time, and the Nanjing Road Business Association and the First District Branch of the Citizens' Association have strongly opposed it. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the four major domestic product groups have jointly opposed it, and their expressions are stronger than before. Therefore, although the board of directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council still allowed the price increase, it failed to pass the "per-call calculation plan." However, users have received unofficial news from the company that the company is still determined to increase prices on a per-call basis and is currently using various methods to promote its success. The Nanjing Road Business Association and the First District Branch of the Citizens' Association have already found the 12.5% increase in telephone prices unbearable. Per-call calculation would be more than three or four times higher. They have surveyed the number of telephone calls used by their members and received reports from 93 companies with 150 telephone lines. Six lines make 270 calls per day, four lines make 130 calls, one line makes 103 calls, eight lines make 100 calls, two lines make 75 calls, one line makes 70 calls, four lines make 60 calls, one line makes 55 calls, six lines make 50 calls, three lines make 45 calls, ten lines make 40 calls, four lines make 33 calls, 26 lines make 30 calls, four lines make 25 calls, 28 lines make 110 calls, ten lines make 15 calls, eleven lines make 10 calls, and 21 lines make less than 10 calls. The above numbers are recorded separately every day from April 1 to 7 and averaged out, which is very accurate. According to this, most people make 20 to 30 calls per day. If the price is increased based on the number of calls, it will exceed the original price by more than one time, and even those who make less than 10 calls will increase by more than 12.5%. Not to mention those who make more than 30 calls per day. Therefore, the two associations have officially released the above survey statistics to arouse the attention of general users. In addition to expressing their opposition, they will send a letter to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, asking the Chinese directors attending the Shanghai Municipal Council to pay close attention and not to blindly follow the Western directors' approval of the telephone company's unlimited profits due to the telephone company's deceptive petitions, so as to increase the burden on the citizens and hinder the development of transportation.

Honors of Painter Chang Shuhong

Painter Chang Shuhong has studied in France for seven years. He has studied at the Lyon School of Fine Arts and the Paris School of Fine Arts, achieving excellent results and gaining fame overseas. He has won awards at the Lyon Salon and the Paris Salon. This spring, his three works, "Patient," "Family Portrait," and "Woman Portrait," were exhibited at the Lyon Spring Salon and won the first-place gold medal. At the same time, he was selected as a super-selected member by the Lyon Artists Association, which means that his works will not be subject to review in the future and can participate in the spring Salon at any time (i.e., HC). Recently, he participated in the Paris National Student Art Exhibition, and his work "Still Life" was personally selected by the Vice Minister of Fine Arts of the French Ministry of Education, Yu Yisimen, to be purchased by the state. Previously, Mr. Chang's "Nude Woman" was purchased by the French government and is now in the Lyon Art Museum for people to admire. This time, he has received such honors again, which is a great honor for the country.

Books and Newspapers Cooperative: Tan Tian Wins Appeal, Fined 100 Yuan

The Kaiming Bookstore and the Books and Newspapers Cooperative competed and publicly accused each other in newspapers due to the printing and distribution of the posthumous works of the late Hanlin scholar Ke Shaomin's New Yuan History. Zhang Xichen, the manager of Kaiming, stated that Tan Tian, the manager of the Books and Newspapers Cooperative, used the terms "general merchants" and "omissions and errors" in an advertisement published on January 28, which was actually scolding Kaiming. Zhang then filed a criminal lawsuit against Tan Tian for copyright infringement and public defamation through his lawyer, Sun Zuji. The First Special District Court initially ruled that the copyright infringement part was rejected, and the defamation part was determined that "merchant" was indeed a scolding term and was unwilling to accept the decision. His defense lawyer, Li Mo, submitted an appeal, citing various commentaries and books on the interpretation of the word "merchant," stating that it had no meaning of defamation and was not specifically referring to Kaiming with the term "merchant." Therefore, it was difficult to accept the original judgment. On the afternoon of last Monday, Qian Hongye, the presiding judge of the First Special Court's Criminal Division, together with two judges, Wu Tingqi and Wu Zehan, specially opened a collegial panel to summon both parties, investigate evidence, and conduct the statutory procedures of statements and debates. The verdict was announced in court yesterday afternoon. The main text was "The original judgment is revoked, Tan Tian publicly insulted others and is fined 100 yuan, and the remaining part of the defamation lawsuit is acquitted."

Cai Songchun and Others Acquitted

The woman Chen Jiangshi, previously because after becoming pregnant, she had bleeding from time to time, still went to Cai Songchun and Cai Baichun, national physicians specializing in women's medicine, at No. 5 Gu Shan Lane, Xihuaide Road, Hongkou, for diagnosis and treatment. Later, Chen had a miscarriage, believing that it was caused by the herbs prescribed by Cai, including Ze Xie and Tong Cao. She then brought the lawsuit to the First Special District Court, requesting that they be punished for the crime of negligent injury. The Special District Court repeatedly summoned the Cai’s, who claimed that Chen's miscarriage was caused by lifting heavy objects. The court sent the prescription to the Shanghai National Medicine Association for determination. The result was that Cai's prescription was not mistaken, and Cai also presented various gynecology medical books to prove the appropriateness of using Ban Xia and Tong Cao, and hired lawyers to defend them. After the interrogation was over, the details have been detailed in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiang Yinghua opened the ninth criminal court and announced the verdict, the main text being that Cai Songchun and Cai Baichun were acquitted.

Yuanxing Steamer Aground at Shierxu, Hull Deeply Stuck in Shoal, Already Unloading Cargo

The Yuanxing Company's Yuanxing steamer, managed by Dakang, is a "wild flag" vessel, loading cargo everywhere. This time, it was fully loaded with coal from Pukou, Nanjing, bound for Shanghai. It left Pukou on the evening of the 7th. That night, it reached the waters of Shierxu near Zhenjiang. Due to poor weather conditions and fog on the river, it mistakenly sailed into a shoal and the hull ran aground.

Unable to Escape

After the accident, the shipowner tried to get out of the shoal by running the engines at full power and reversing, but the ship was fully loaded with coal and the hull was very heavy. The hull was deeply stuck in the sand, and all kinds of methods failed to move it even a bit. He had no choice but to urgently telegraph Shanghai for help yesterday morning (the 8th).

Unloading Cargo

Upon receiving the news, the Yuanxing Company immediately discussed and decided to unload the cargo from the ship in order to reduce the load and make the rescue easier. It immediately telegraphed the Zhenjiang agency to hire tugs and barges to unload the cargo from the hold first, so that the hull could float, and then tow it away at high tide.

Reporting to All Parties

The Yuanxing steamer has a load capacity of over 1,000 tons and has peace insurance with the Shanghai Ship Insurance Association. Yesterday, it sent a letter to the insurance company, stating that the company's Yuanxing steamer ran aground in the waters of Shierxu last night (the 7th) while loading cargo from Pukou, Nanjing, bound for Shanghai. A telegram has been sent to Shanghai this morning (the 8th). The company immediately telegraphed Zhenjiang, ordering the agency to quickly unload the cargo and then seek towing assistance. The shipowner's original telegram was attached. (The rest omitted.)

Chamber of Commerce Submits to Ministry of Finance, Requesting Exemption from New Jade Export Tax

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that on the 5th of this month, the Municipal Antique Industry Association stated in a letter that the association had received a letter from new jade members, stating that since the Shanghai War, all domestic industries have been in decline and international trade has been sluggish. The important reason is the economic panic and the dynamics of the times. As a result, foreign trade has plummeted, and the number of imports has increased day by day, which cannot be curbed. Exports have decreased sharply. The new jade industry is even worse. New jade relies entirely on sales to Europe and the United States and is classified as a cultural plaything. The number is very small and was not worth paying attention to. In recent years, it has become even more depressed. The reason is the high cost. The raw materials for these items are minerals, and all rely on handmade polishing to imitate ancient manufacturing equipment, resulting in slow production and a sharp increase in the number of living indexes, which make the tax rate heavier. Although they try to lower the value, sales are still small. Merchants in this industry are barely surviving. If there is no speedy relief to restore the original foreign trade situation, then society will inevitably increase the number of unemployed people by the thousands, and the country will also lose one type of export trade and production. If the country and society suffer major losses, they are now trying to seek self-relief to reduce the accumulated costs, and ask them to submit a document to the Ministry of Finance to verify and exempt the export tax rate in order to maintain livelihoods. The association believes that what the new jade members are requesting is indeed the truth. Therefore, it is submitting a detailed account of the commercial difficulties, and requesting the Ministry of Finance to follow the precedent of verifying and exempting the export tax on domestic products such as ivory, carpets, porcelain, and cloisonné, and to approve the request to verify and exempt the export tax rate on new jade in order to maintain industrial and commercial foreign trade, so as to passively reduce imports and actively prevent unemployment. Industry and commerce are fortunate, and the country is fortunate, and await orders. After receiving the letter, the association found that it had issued several opinions on cutting and writing off transit taxes and reducing and exempting export taxes in order to alleviate the massive imports and reverse the industrial and commercial recession. The new jade item is sold to Europe and the United States because it is classified as a cultural toy. The sales volume is not high, but because the makers all rely on hand polishing, which takes a long time, there are still many workers who rely on it for their livelihoods. In recent years, under the influence of the world's economic recession, this industry has also been in decline. It is even more necessary to exempt taxes and reduce costs in order to save it. The types of goods that the industry requested to be exempted from export tax this time are all kinds of jade, all kinds of crystal stones, all kinds of agate, all kinds of powder jade, coral fluorite and other ornaments, and various unfinished jade stones. According to the current export tax, all are taxed at a rate of 7.05 per hundred from the price, the burden is heavy, and sales are not good. According to the letter, it is practical and convenient to handle.

Traveling in Sheng: Zhou Lingfa from Ningbo Falsely Accused and Detained; Fellow Townsmen Associations in Ningbo and Dinghai Seek Redress

Zhou Lingfa, a native of Dinghai residing in Shengshan, Chongming County, is 52 years old. He engages in the fishing industry and runs a Tongxiang grocery store. He enjoys a good reputation in the Shengshan business community and enthusiastically supports local public welfare. As a result, he has been envied by some petty people who falsely accused him to the Jiangsu Provincial Government of being involved in a drug trafficking operation in Dagangshan Dahang, Shengshan. After investigation by officials sent by the provincial government, no suspicion was found, confirming that he was framed. Yang Youcai, Gu Youfa, and many Shengshan merchants, who were also implicated in the false accusation, provided signed affidavits to the provincial government. On the 24th of last month, Deng Hui, a special agent of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters in Shanghai, reinvestigated the case and detained Zhou Lingfa. Merchants in Shengshan, believing Zhou Lingfa to be a legitimate businessman, sent a telegram to the Ningbo Association in Shanghai, requesting assistance in seeking redress. The association, upon learning the situation and noting Zhou Lingfa's origin from Dinghai, decided to jointly petition the Songhu Garrison Headquarters with the Dinghai Association in Shanghai, requesting a swift and clear investigation and release of the innocent, to alleviate the injustice.

Special Report

Jin Cheng Bank's Business Report for 1934

— (26)

Category Number Type Loan Amount

Agriculture 830 12 types 12,359 yuan

Industry 850 124 industries 18,291 yuan

Commerce 2,145 118 industries 31,107 yuan

(Note) The above loan amounts range from 1 yuan to 200 yuan.

The average loan per household is 16 yuan.

In addition, the bank's total loan amount in that area is limited to 200 yuan, which is not enough to meet the needs of society. Therefore, a special small loan category was established, with amounts ranging from 200 yuan to 1,000 yuan. This year, the total amount of loans issued was 120,920 yuan, with a total of 193 borrowers. 53,325 yuan has been successively recovered. As of the end of the year, the actual outstanding balance was 67,595 yuan, with 161 actual borrowers.

Most of the above small loans and small-amount loans can be repaid as agreed when due, which shows that the people of our country respect credit and that the loans can be used for production and to assist where necessary.

B. Assisting the Rural Economy

The revitalization of the rural economy is an urgent task today. The whole country is discussing ways to promote it. Considering the vast territory of our country, the many improvements that should be made in agriculture, and the complexity of its related situation, the bank is a commercial bank. How dare it say that it has made a contribution? However, since this matter concerns the foundation of the country, it can only do what it can, and work with various social organizations to make considerable efforts in research and partial implementation to assist in every possible way. The details of this year's work are listed below: (1) The organization of the North China Agricultural Research and Improvement Association. The association is jointly organized by the bank, Tianjin Nankai University, and the Ding County Mass Education Promotion Association. It is divided into research and implementation departments, working together to improve cotton production, which occupies an important position in Hebei's agricultural products and has a special relationship in our country's economy. Therefore, it will start with this. The research work is to improve quality, establish breeding grounds, and investigate the production and sales situation in various places to facilitate improvement. The implementation work is to regulate finance and promote transportation and sales, such as providing production loans, establishing warehouses, and handling mortgages in Ding, Zhao, Li Jin, Nangong, Wuji, Shulu and other places, guiding the organization of cooperatives, etc. As a result, the cotton production of various cooperatives is still able to be sold at higher prices than usual, increasing the direct income of cotton farmers. It is estimated that each bale earns an additional profit of 2 to 4 yuan. Although the amount is small, by analogy, if the scope is gradually expanded, it seems that it will be beneficial to the rural economy.

(2) The organization of joint loans for cotton production and marketing cooperatives in Shaanxi, Henan, and Shanxi. In June of the third year, the bank joined with five other banks in the same industry to regulate the cotton production finance of the three provinces of Shaanxi, Henan, and Shanxi. The Shaanxi Cotton Production Improvement Institute was entrusted to organize cotton production and marketing cooperatives in the three provinces and act as an agent for the banks to issue funds. The cooperatives were managed separately for production loans, transportation loans, and sales loans.

In addition, the bank or its affiliates invest in or operate packing plants and cotton ginning plants related to the production and marketing of agricultural products, such as those in Zhengzhou, Xi'an, Lingbao, Zhangde, and Nantong. (To be continued)

Free Talk

On "Scholars Despising Each Other" (1)

— Cao Juren

"Our family's" Zihuan, 1,800 years ago, said the phrase "Scholars despise each other, it has been so since ancient times," which has been used by some people as a defense and explanation for "personal attacks." Sometimes, when so-called scholars are seen "scolding each other," it is said to be "scholars despising each other," and all serious criticism is lumped together with "despising," thinking that criticism is the same as scolding. It seems that "our family's" Zihuan did not say it that way.

In his essay "Dian Lun Lun Wen," after the sentence "Scholars despise each other, it has been so since ancient times," he immediately mentioned Ban Gu's criticism of Fu Yi, saying, "Wu Zhong (Fu Yi's courtesy name) was able to write, and was the order of the Lantai, but could not stop his pen. Ban Gu said that Fu Yi "could not stop his pen," which was a technical criticism. So Zihuan explained the reason for "despising each other," saying: "People are abundant in self-view, and writing is not of one form, and few can be fully virtuous. Therefore, each despises what they are short in with what they are long in." Later, he talked about the Seven Masters of Jian'an, and said: "These seven masters, there is nothing left in learning, and nothing borrowed in words. All ride their steeds for thousands of miles, and look up to stride side by side. It is very difficult to subdue each other with this!" Strictly speaking, "scholars despising each other" is only a kind of "criticism" and does not contain the meaning of "scolding each other."

I am now presumptuously acting as a confidant and elaborating on the meaning of what "our family's" Zihuan called "scholars despising each other."

Liu Xie said, "People's talents are different in speed... Those who are quick to develop their talents have a good grasp of the key techniques, are quick to think ahead, and make decisive decisions; those who think deeply have many paths in their emotions, are aware after doubts, and are determined after research. Because of their quick thinking, they succeed hastily, and because of their doubt, they achieve results over time." (Wen Xin Diao Long: Shen Si). For example, Sima Xiangru wrote Shanglin Zixu, focusing his attention and effort, and it took almost a hundred days to succeed. The eldest son of Huang Zu hosted a shooting competition for guests, and someone offered a parrot: She asked Mi Heng to write a poem, and Mi Heng wrote it with a pen, "The writing was flawless and the words were beautiful." Between these two poets, the difference in speed was so great, who is higher and who is lower? Han Wu Story recorded: "The emperor (Emperor Wu of Han) liked lyrics and poems. Whenever he traveled and saw strange beasts and objects, he would order Xiangru to write poems about them. The emperor himself also wrote hundreds of poems, which he completed with a pen and did not think about them beforehand. Xiangru took a long time to create writing, and the emperor was always pleased with his craftsmanship. He said to Xiangru, "Can I exchange my speed for your slowness?" Xiangru said, "It is possible for me, but I do not know how your majesty would feel?" The emperor laughed loudly and did not blame him." Between these monarchs and ministers, one slow and one fast, each was a little self-satisfied and did not give in to each other. Western Capital Miscellaneous Records said: "Mei Gao's articles were quick and agile, and Zhang Qing's production was slow and delayed. Both exhausted the praise of the time. However, Zhang Qing's beginning and end were gentle and beautiful, and Mei Gao's sometimes had clumsy sentences. Therefore, we know that quick travel has no good traces." The words showed quite a bit of respect for Xiangru. And the author of Records of the Three Kingdoms, Chen Shou, praised Wang Can: "He composed with a pen and did not make any changes. People at the time often thought that it was a pre-existing structure. However, even if it was deeply thought out, it could not be added." He praised Cao Zhi for composing Copper Sparrow Terrace Fu "lifting his pen and completing it, and it was worth seeing." Also deeply admired. There are clearly these two different methods between writers, so it is easy to "despise what they are short in with what they are long in."

The emphasis on form and content among writers has been a very divided debate in almost every era. Pei Ziye, a great historian of the Qi and Liang dynasties, wrote An Essay on Carving Insects, opposing the literary trend of taking decoration as ability, saying: "Young boys and girls, nobles and children, all do not abandon the six arts, chanting sentiments. Scholars take broad dependence as an urgent task, saying that chapters and sentences are narrow and stupid, and indulging in literature and breaking the classics is a success, which is not covered by musical instruments, and is not only about etiquette and righteousness... Their excitement is superficial, their ambition is weak, skillful but not important, hidden but not deep... Xun Qing said, 'A sign of a chaotic era is that writing is hidden and out of touch.' Is this not close to it?" Emperor Jianwen of Liang was not happy when he saw it, and replied to King Xiangdong: "Now there are those who imitate Xie Kangle, and Pei Honglu (Ziye)'s writings are also quite confusing. Why? Xie Ke's words are naturally pulled out of the sky, and there are times when he is not constrained, which is his dross. Pei is a talented historian, with no beauty in his writing. To learn Xie is not to reach its essence, but only to get its length; to learn Pei is to abandon its strengths, and only get its weaknesses. Xie is so clever that he cannot be climbed, and Pei is so qualitative that he should not be admired... Therefore, jade emblems and gold chisels are ridiculed by clumsy eyes, and the Lower Lane of Ba people is more suitable for the listening of Yingzhong. The spring is high and not harmonious, and the wonderful sound is cut off and not sought. After all, without careful discussion, weighing the quality of writing, there is a different skill, and finally ashamed of the beautiful hand. Therefore, scholars who hold jade retreat when they see Zheng, and people who wear Zhangfu and jade shoes sigh when they look at Minxiang. Poetry is like this, and writing is also like this, only because the ink is silent, it is driven and dyed, and the paper is ruthless, it is allowed to shake and fold. How great, the horizontal flow of writing, has reached this point!" Such a sharp and contrasting one knife, one gun, is quite beautiful. In addition, between the two, there is a third hero who came out, Yan Zhitui in the article chapter said: "Today's world inherits and abandons the end, and they all float with dust. Words compete with reason, and words win and reason is suppressed. Things compete with talent, and things are complex and talent is damaged. The dissolute flow away and forget to return, and the chisellers patch and are insufficient. The times are like this, how can we alone violate it, but we must go to the extreme. There must be a great talent and reputation to reform the style, which is what I hope for." Li Yanshou's preface to Northern History Literary Garden Biography said: "And in the Yongming Tianjian period, between the Taihe Tianbao, Luoyang Jiangzuo, literature and elegance were especially prosperous. The preferences of each other are quite different. Jiangzuo palace music is developed and more valuable than Qingqi; Hebei's words and meanings are chaste and strong, and more important than temperament. Temperament then reason wins over words, Qingqi then literature exceeds its meaning. Those who win with reason are convenient for the times, and those who are literary are suitable for singing songs. This is the general difference between the gains and losses of northern and southern lyricists. If they can receive his Qing sound, simplify his tired sentences, each remove their short, combine their strengths, then literature and quality will be refined, and all beauty will be perfect." This argument of equal emphasis on form and content can also be said to be a kind of scholar's mutual contempt.

Loving Through Hating

— Long Gonggong

Once, in an essay by a writer, there was a main argument that said: "...All the great writers in the world, past and present, are humanists. They hate the ignorant masses, the more they hate them, the more they love them, and when they hate them to the point of no return, they give their lives to save them..." The most interesting slogan was: "They hate to love, and love to hate!" The original text has been remembered vaguely, and the above quote is only an approximation, but that slogan will never be forgotten.

If a talented man loves a beautiful woman, and the beautiful woman ignores him, then the talented man hates her to the bone. This is purely "hating to love" and is easy to understand.

But I don't understand how to "love through hating" – how unimaginable that is! Later, after reading Gorky's "Reminiscences of Tolstoy," I found a barely similar character in the article "The Shepherd."

The shepherd Dingtai Botzuofu is "a man with a complete soul. He is smart, upright, lives a life of moderation, and is very cheerful. He is over sixty years old, but his body is still fat and strong, with a broad chest and a bronze complexion." He is a philosopher. He scolds education.

"Why do humans have to live separately? Because of education. Education separates me and you, preventing us from understanding each other... Everyone calls the children to a place to gather, and for several years, they teach them some troubles... How can education be given to everyone? There will not be so much education in the world!... Knowing the law: Don't take things that don't belong to you, be careful of your own property, don't eat all the food, you should leave some for the dog, wear warm clothes, believe in God - you see, this is what a good person knows. This is the education that good people need most..." People who have been educated are all crazy people, people with confused minds."

He often said such things. He determined that the thing that caused problems among human beings was education; ridiculed the landlord's son Mi Jia for wearing glasses and catching butterflies, collecting golden beetles and grass leaves all day long, preparing to write a book about the life of insects (this educated man also said that mosquitoes spread fever, advising him to be careful); because a teacher used his position as a teacher to tell the children that the emperor was the cause of all suffering, he scolded the teacher: "If he is not a beast, he must be a fool. He is a cow."

But later Gorky learned that "this shepherd has two fatherless and motherless nephews, who are both studying, and the shepherd is paying for it, one at the Veterinary School in Kazan, and one at the Middle School in Ulady," so when he went to question him, he said in a low voice:

"My nephews are related to me by blood. You are just an outsider, like a traveling beggar, as the world says. So I act for my own benefit in the way that all mentally sound people do. I want my people to be educated, but I don't want others to be educated... Do you understand? This is... Everyone says: Whether you want to or not, relatives are still relatives. So I use myself to help my own relatives. Do you believe that I don't want to see them become decent gentlemen?... "

This Mr. Dingtai Botzuofu can probably be said to hate education to the extreme, and then he loved it, wanting to monopolize education, which is a bit like "loving through hating."

Youth

— Li Sanlang

Is my youth forever buried with the passing time in silence?

However, this dark journey has long ruined the pure heart that had not yet left my childhood.

During the day, I seek my meager nourishment alone with a hurried tune; in the evening, the streets are so cold and I return with a tired body, quietly meditating and writing in that same small house filled with the depressing smell of misfortune, spending the desolate night so regularly from seven o'clock to two o'clock after midnight. This time is most suitable for working, and I rarely let it be blown away with the howling wind outside the window. When the young dancer living in the front building returns with heavy steps, it is two o'clock after midnight. The faint and distant urban rooster is crowing, as if urging me not to spend the cold night like this and ruin my youth.

—It is time to go to sleep.

However, I lie in bed, my heavy head so habitually stirring up scenes of thought - in the childhood of seven or eight years old, living in the quiet countryside, hearing such a crowing sound, the sky was still dim, and the people in the countryside quickly got up and waited for the beautiful sun to rise in the east. Later, I moved to the city and rarely heard the crowing of roosters. Now, I am living such an abnormal life—I only go to sleep when the crane crows.

Tired body, in the small cloth bed, in the sturdy quilt that has wandered with me for so long. Thinking of all kinds of darkness and indignation in the world, thinking of how I should resolutely pursue the path of great light, thinking of how I should use my pen to depict the people who are living a painful life in the circle of darkness. At that time, my head was stimulated and very excited, like madly rushing out of the dark night to find everything we needed. Gradually, I passed the short night that was about to dawn, dimly and trembling. At eight o'clock in the morning, the arrogant voice of the city awakened me again, so constantly passing these boring days.

However, I need the gentle and tender red morning sun. I am not willing to bury my youth in the silent circle forever.

A Village Woman's Night

— Ding Lang

The sound of crying,

Ripples through the tattered cotton wadding;

Yearning for her mother's milk.

The lamplight spills on her hands,

Needle and thread try to capture the fleeing night,

A flurry of busyness!

The cold wind creeps in through the door cracks,

Making the flame flicker,

Exhaustion wrings out her husband's snores,

Tilling the fields has drained his spirit,

Her eyes glance over,

And a hardened heart urges on her own toil!

Visiting the Sick

— Yier

Knowing full well that visiting hours for ordinary hospital patients only start at three in the afternoon, I always arrive at the hospital by half past two. It’s not that I’m impatient, but standing and waiting aimlessly at the hospital entrance, letting those long thirty minutes, second by second, drive me crazy, is something I really can’t bear. But why do I go early? There’s a reason for my early arrival. I feel that even though I’m anxious waiting outside, inside room number twenty-one of the hospital, there's a very seriously ill patient who, during the twenty-four hours of the day, is even more anxiously awaiting the arrival of three o’clock in the afternoon, and hoping that I’ll visit her and give her a little comfort! Moreover, waiting while standing at the hospital entrance is much better than sitting at home waiting. Because arriving at the hospital a little earlier and looking inside from the outside feels like seeing her a little earlier, and my heart feels a lot lighter. Therefore, I am very willing to endure this half-hour of pain every day, not daring to arrive even a little later.

Time passes minute by minute with the shadow of the sun on the ground, and people visiting patients arrive one after another. Some mothers visit their daughters, some husbands visit their wives, and some friends visit friends. Each visitor brings more or less some food, such as side dishes, biscuits, fruit, and milk. The feelings of these people are different. Those with faces full of sorrow, one can tell at a glance that the patients they are visiting are in very serious condition. Those with joyful expressions between their brows and eyes undoubtedly have relatives who are already on the mend and no longer need medicine. As for the few who are visiting new mothers, they mostly look very happy. Perhaps some of them are happy to be fathers, and some are happy to be grandfathers or grandmothers.

Every day when I go to the hospital, I also bring some things as usual: oranges, bread, and ham. In addition, I carry a heavy heart. Every day because I arrive early, I first put the things on the table in the gatehouse, put my hands in the left and right pockets of my coat, and pace back and forth outside the gate alone. At this time, nothing but extremely terrifying shadows emerge. Before my eyes is her gray, pale, and thin face, and in my ears are her intermittent and miserable cries. However, unreliable wishful thinking is not absent either. Perhaps after taking the medicine, she is a little better today? Perhaps after the injection, she is now sleeping comfortably? Perhaps the vomiting has stopped, and she can eat? However, among these many "perhaps," there is another "perhaps" that I dare not imagine, which is: perhaps she has unfortunately… Thinking like this, three o’clock finally arrives. As soon as the gate opens, the group of people standing at the gate rush in like a tide. As soon as I step into the gate, my heart becomes confused and uneasy. The closer I get to the ward, the faster my heart beats. Room number twenty-one is already in front of me. I walk in in one breath, open my flustered eyes, look at the patient lying on the bed, and the first thing I say is: "How are you today?" If the answer is: "A little better!" my heart feels like a lead weight has been lifted, and immediately calms down! If she holds my hand and sobs sadly, then my heart feels like it's being stabbed with a knife, and I instantly feel an unusual ache!

Two hours pass in a flash, and we have to separate temporarily again. I reluctantly leave this patient in the quiet hospital and walk home alone. Meeting again after twenty-two hours feels farther away than a year; it’s really hard to wait! What makes me most uneasy is: what state will she be in tomorrow?

Mr. Ju Qing (10)

— Ke Ling

What makes him slightly dissatisfied now is that group of students, obviously of varying quality. Strict control was originally Mr. Ju Qing's only educational principle, but now this principle is gradually becoming somewhat ineffective. The students transferred from the district primary school are invariably naughty, love to make trouble, are good at causing mischief, and do not submit to the teacher's control: as long as Mr. Ju Qing leaves the study for even a step, there will immediately be disputes, adding much annoyance to his life.

This academic atmosphere should be rectified, he thought.

Among the newly arrived students, the most stubborn and recalcitrant is Shen Qingzhong. This child spends almost all of his time playing naughty games and can barely sit still for a moment. Since he arrived, it seems that many students have been influenced by him and have become restless. To make an example of one to warn a hundred, Mr. Ju Qing decided to start rectifying the academic atmosphere with this child.

However, the strict management method that Mr. Ju Qing has used effectively for twenty years has lost its effectiveness on Shen Qingzhong.

This child's mischievousness seems to be innate, and his temperament is as tough as rawhide glue. Every time he is found to have broken the rules and is brought before him, he stands in front of you like a wooden stake. No matter how much you scold him, how harshly and loudly you rebuke him, he always clenches his teeth and stubbornly refuses to open his mouth. As soon as you finish scolding him, he turns around and immediately sticks out his tongue and makes faces at his classmates. Back in his seat, he still secretly engages in his naughty deeds, and even if you make him kneel in front of Confucius's spirit tablet, he will grin and giggle with a shameless face.

As a last resort, Mr. Ju Qing decided to use the corporal punishment of his greatest authority.
