Sports News

The Sixth National Games Preparatory Committee Held Its First Meeting Yesterday, Appointing Chairman Lin and Chairman Jiang, Among Others, as Honorary Presidents, Deciding on the Candidates for the Competition and Judging Committees, and Stipulating the Deadline for Submitting the List of Participating Events from Various Regions, and the First Meeting of the Preparatory Committee Will Be Held This Friday, and the Overall Championship Will Be Maintained

The Sixth National Games, scheduled to be held in the downtown area of the city on this year's Double Tenth Festival, the Preparatory Committee held its first meeting at the City Hall meeting room at 12:00 noon yesterday to discuss various arrangements. The details are as follows:

Attending Committee Members

Wang Shijie, Chu Minyi, Wang Zhengting (represented by Shen Siliang), Zhang Boling, Wu Tiecheng, Yu Hongjun, Pan Gongzhan, Chen Kuisheng (represented by Jiang Xiangqing), Song Ruhai, Yang Hu (represented by Wang Chengzhi), Cai Jingjun, Cai Zengji, Xu Peihuang, Li Ting'an, Shen Yi, Dong Dayou, Hao Gengsheng, Zhang Jiong, Lei Zhen, Xu Yiqiao, Tong Xingbai, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng (represented by Wang Xiaolai), Shen Siliang, Yuan Dunli, Wu Yunrui, Ma John, Xu Minhui, Cheng Dengke, Pan Youqiang (represented by Cheng Dengke), Jiang Xiangqing, Chen Yongxing, Li Dachao, Ma Chonggan, Shao Rugan, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Shizhen (represented by Wu Yunrui), etc.

Chairman's Report

Chairman Minister Wang, Recorder Wang Daxu, with the formalities observed, first the Chairman reported, briefly stating that today's first preparatory meeting for the Sixth National Games is being held in Shanghai. According to the decision of the Executive Yuan, the National Games are held every four years in rotation between the central government and various provinces and cities, that is, this committee meets every two years, once in the central government and the next time in the provinces and cities. This year the conference is being held in Shanghai for two reasons: (1) Because the Shanghai Municipality proposed it after the last conference, in order to promote the construction of a sports ground in Greater Shanghai. (2) Because Shanghai Municipality won the championship and had the best results. Now there are only five or six months left before the conference, and the time is extremely pressing. It is hoped that after this meeting, the directors of each group will work hard to prepare and proceed, and that the representatives from remote areas will participate in the representatives, which will increase compared with the previous conference. There are two experiences gained from the last conference: (1) The issue of participating units and the number of people, that is, the principle of popularity. In this session, the participating units and the number of people in remote areas can be increased compared with the previous session. (2) Regarding the issue of funding, it is hoped that this session can achieve the effect of popularity with relatively less expense. The above points are personal feelings and are specially contributed to the members of the preparatory committee for reference.

Mayor's Speech

Next, Mayor Wu delivered a speech, briefly stating that it is a great honor for the Sixth National Games to be held in this city. As for the various preparations, since the Ministry of Education has entrusted them, it is incumbent upon us. However, having undertaken the preparations, I feel deeply afraid, because this city is the gateway to the capital, and my colleagues are humble and inexperienced, and the preparations may be inadequate, so I have to hope that the Central Ministry of Education and everyone will give instructions at any time, so as to serve as a guide.

Honorary Presidents

Then the discussion items, (II) the proposal to appoint honorary presidents and honorary vice presidents, resolved that the conference appoint National Government Chairman Lin Sen as honorary president, and appoint Military Committee Chairman Jiang Zhongzheng, President of the Executive Yuan Wang Zhaoming, President of the Legislative Yuan Sun Ke, President of the Judicial Yuan Ju Zheng, President of the Examination Yuan Dai Chuanxian, President of the Control Yuan Yu Youren, Vice President of the Executive Yuan Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Legislative Yuan Shao Yuanchong, Vice President of the Judicial Yuan Qin Zhen, Vice President of the Examination Yuan Niu Yongjian, Vice President of the Control Yuan Ding Weifen, as honorary vice presidents. (II) The proposal to determine the heads of each group and section, resolved to hand it over to the Standing Committee for determination.

Candidates for the Two Committees

(III) The candidate list for the Competition Committee of this committee, resolved to appoint Wang Zhengting as director, Wang Fudan, Shen Guoquan, Wu Bangwei, Wu Yunrui, Shen Siliang, Shao Rugan, Hao Gengsheng, Ma John, Yuan Dunli, Zhang Boling, Gao Zuo, Chen Yongxing, Chen Kuisheng, Xu Chonghou, Chu Minyi, Cheng Dengke, Jiang Xiangqing as members. (IV) The candidate list for the Judging Committee of this committee, resolved to appoint Zhang Boling as director, Wang Zhengting, Wu Cheng, Wu Bangwei, Wu Yunrui, Shen Siliang, Song Ruhai, Qiu Jixiang, Hao Gengsheng, Zhang Zhijiang, Zhang Huixun, Zhang Zhongfan, Chen Kun, Chen Kuisheng, Xu Minhui, Chu Minshuo, Dong Shouyi, Jiang Xiangqing, Liu Xuesong as members.

Regulations

(V) The proposal on the procedures for the various sections of the Competition Committee, resolved that the matters that should be handled by the various sections of the Competition Committee should be handled in accordance with the orders of the director of the preparatory committee and the general secretary of the conference in order to unify powers. (VI) The proposal to submit the detailed rules of this committee, the competition regulations of the conference, the organizational regulations of the competition committee, the organizational regulations of the judging committee, and the rules of the sports competition of the conference for discussion, resolved to hand it over to the Standing Committee for review and submit it to the next meeting for discussion. (VII) How to proceed with the work plan of each group and section, resolved to designate Committee Member Pan Gongzhan, Committee Member Hao Gengsheng, and Committee Member Shen Siliang to review and submit it to the Standing Committee for discussion.

A photograph of the Preparatory Committee of the Sixth National Games (taken by Wang Kai)

Funding and Other Items

(VIII) The budget proposal for the conference expenses, resolved that the director of the preparatory committee should consult with the Ministry of Education and then submit it to the Executive Yuan for approval. (IX) The proposal on whether to cancel the overall championship of the conference, resolved that the original proposal should be maintained and not cancelled. (X) The proposal on whether to amend the tennis championship competition rules, resolved to hand it over to the original proposer to draft the revised provisions and submit them to the Standing Committee for discussion. (XI) The proposal on the performance events that should be stipulated at the conference of this committee, resolved to hand it over to the Standing Committee to decide and report to the conference. (XII) Send letters to the Ministries of Communications and Railways to reduce or exempt the cost of train and ship tickets for the selected athletes. How to handle the reduction or exemption limit and procedures? Resolved to handle it according to the precedents of the previous session. (XIII) Should international competitions be invited to be held by overseas Chinese in Shanghai after the conference is over? Resolved not to submit it for discussion for the time being. (XIV) The proposal to request that Tai Chi exercises be stipulated as a group performance at the opening ceremony of this conference, resolved and passed.

Registration Date

(XV) The proposal on the deadline for registering the list of participating events and athletes from each province, city, and unit, resolved that the registration for participating events will be closed on September 10, and the registration for the list of participating athletes will be closed at 12:00 noon on September 20. Late registrations will be invalid. (XVI) The proposal to use the scoring method to rank the overall championship of the conference, resolved to hand it over to the Standing Committee for deliberation. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

The first meeting of the Standing Committee of the Preparatory Committee will be held at 9:30 a.m. on the 12th of this month (Friday) in the City Hall meeting room. In addition to the members of the Standing Committee, the Deputy General Secretaries must also attend. Education News

Ministry of Education Revised and Promulgated Two Regulations on Graduation Examinations for Secondary School and Normal School Students (II)

(II) Regulations for Graduation Examinations of Normal School Students

Article 1: The education administrative organs of each province, city, and district shall conduct graduation examinations for graduating students of all types of normal schools and normal departments under their jurisdiction after the original schools have examined and verified that their graduation scores are passing. Private normal schools and normal departments of all types that have been filed with the Ministry shall participate in the graduation examinations for normal school students in their respective provinces and cities.

Article 2: The graduation examinations of all types of normal schools and normal departments in provinces, counties, and cities shall be organized and handled by committees organized by the education administrative organs of each province.

The graduation examinations of all types of normal schools and normal departments in cities (municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan) and districts (special administrative regions) (excluding those established by the province) shall be organized and handled by committees organized by the education administrative organs of the respective cities and districts.

Article 3: The Regulations for Committees for Graduation Examinations of Normal School Students shall apply to the Regulations for Committees for Graduation Examinations of Secondary School Students.

The aforementioned examination committee may be organized jointly with the Committee for Graduation Examinations of Secondary School Students, and its name shall be the Committee for Graduation Examinations of Secondary School and Normal School Students of a certain province (city or district).

Article 4: The subjects for the graduation examination of normal schools or normal departments are stipulated as follows:

1. Normal Schools: Civics, Chinese Language, Arithmetic, Physics, Chemistry, Biology, History, Geography, Introduction to Education, Educational Psychology, Elementary School Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods.

2. Rural Normal Schools: Subjects are the same as normal schools, with the addition of Rural Economy and Cooperation, and Rural Education. Chemistry) Biology (Zoology and Botany) History and Geography (History and Geography) Introduction to Education, Educational Psychology, Elementary School Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods.

3. Simple Rural Normal Schools: Subjects are the same as simple normal schools, with the addition of Rural Economy and Cooperative Rural Education.

4. Three-year and two-year kindergarten normal departments: Civics, Chinese Language, Arithmetic, History, Geography, Biology, Physics, Chemistry, Education Theory, Child Psychology, Kindergarten Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods, Childcare Law.

For the examination subjects of the above categories of normal schools and normal departments, those with the same name and corresponding content and level may be combined for testing.

Article 5: The final semester examination for graduating students of schools participating in the examination shall be held within two weeks before the date of the examination.

Article 6: One month before the examination is held in each place, each school shall submit a roster of graduating students with photos to the competent education administrative authority. The transcript of graduation scores for each subject shall also be submitted before the start of the examination.

Article 7: The method for calculating the scores for each subject in the graduation examination shall be based on the school's graduation scores for each subject (i.e., the average of the scores for each academic year) accounting for 40%, and the scores for each subject in the examination accounting for 60%, combined for calculation.

The aforementioned scores shall be calculated using the percentage method, and 60 points shall be the passing standard.

Article 8: Local graduation examinations shall be held within the last week of June and the first week of January each year. The examination locations shall be determined and announced by the competent education administrative authority. In areas with a wider area and a larger number of students, the examination shall be conducted in districts for the convenience of students, but it shall still be held in accordance with the stipulated dates.

The questions used in the examination shall be formulated by the question-setting committee of the examination committee, and the examination papers shall be prepared by the competent education administrative authority and sealed.

Article 9: Students must pass all subjects in the graduation examination to graduate. The graduation certificate shall be issued by the school after being stamped and sealed by the provincial and municipal education administrative authority with the "Graduation Examination Passed" mark.

Article 10: Students who fail three or more subjects in the examination shall be required to repeat the grade. Those who cannot repeat the grade for reasons may be given a certificate of study by the original school, stating the scores of each subject in the graduation examination, and stamped with a "Graduation Examination Failed" round mark.

Article 11: Students who fail one or two subjects in the examination shall be allowed to continue to participate in the examination of the relevant subjects twice in the next two sessions. They may graduate only after passing. If they still fail any subject, they shall take all the examination subjects.

During the examination, if a student is unable to take all or part of the examination subjects due to any reason, the missed subjects shall be regarded as failing.

Article 12: Students who fail one or two subjects in the examination shall be allowed to work temporarily, and shall only be qualified for formal service after participating in the examination of the relevant subjects and obtaining a graduation certificate.

Article 13: If a student who fails one or two subjects in the examination goes to work in another province or city, the student may request the original school to request the competent education administrative authority to forward the request to the competent education administrative authority where the student is working, allowing him to participate in the local graduation examination and retake the examination for the relevant subjects.

Article 14: The education administrative organs of each province, city, and district shall announce the results of the examination within two weeks after the examination, and issue a certificate of passing the graduation examination.

Article 15: At the end of the examination, the average of the scores of each subject in the graduation examination obtained by each student shall be ranked and announced separately.

At the same time, the percentage of the number of graduating students from each school participating in the examination shall be divided into four grades: A, B, C, and D. Then, the average score of the students passing the examination from each school shall be divided into four grades: A, B, C, and D, and announced.

Article 16: The order of graduation of students from each school shall be arranged by the competent education administrative authority according to the graduation examination scores of each student in each subject.

Article 17: Before holding the graduation examination for normal school students, the education administrative organs of each province, city, and district shall submit the examination location, the list of committee members, and the handling procedures to the Ministry of Education for record. Within one month after the end of the examination, the student examination scores and the grades of the participating schools, as well as the handling process, shall be submitted for record.

Article 18: The education administrative organs of each province, city, and district shall ensure strict confidentiality in handling the graduation examination for normal school students. If there is any leakage of examination questions or other fraudulent behavior, they shall be punished according to law.

Article 19: The education administrative organs of each province, city, and district shall strictly verify the school graduation scores of each student participating in the examination. If any fraudulent behavior is found, all or part of their scores shall be denied, and the responsible personnel shall be disciplined.

Article 20: Graduating students of various normal schools or normal departments not listed in Article 4 shall also take the examination. The examination subjects shall be determined by the competent education administrative authority with reference to the provisions of Article 4.

Article 21: These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Director Wu Broadcasts Speech: Reading Movement and the Chinese Revolution

The National Reading Movement Conference, sponsored by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association, began yesterday. Chen Lifu, chairman of the association, gave the opening speech of the National Reading Movement Conference at the Nanjing Central Broadcasting Station. In Shanghai, Wu Xingya, director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, gave a speech on "Reading Movement and the Chinese Revolution" at the Sino-Western Radio Station from 3:01 PM to 3:30 PM yesterday afternoon. The full text of his speech is as follows:

Wu's Speech: Ladies and gentlemen, recently, the Chinese Cultural Construction Association launched a national reading movement. The publicity in newspapers and the response from all walks of life are truly remarkable, and a reading atmosphere has quickly formed. I believe that this movement is a very valuable movement in the process of the Chinese revolution. Today, the Cultural Construction Association asked me to broadcast, so I will discuss the topic of "Reading Movement and the Chinese Revolution" with everyone.

The current stage of the Chinese revolution, as we all know, is the period of political tutelage from a political perspective, and the period of construction from an economic perspective. The meaning of political tutelage is to train the people to exercise political power and complete Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Principle of Democracy. The meaning of construction is to promote national economic facilities and improve the people's economic lives, completing Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Principle of People's Livelihood. This work is the most difficult and most important in the process of the revolution. We must complete this work in order to guarantee the glory of past revolutionary movements and to achieve the success of future revolutionary movements. Unfortunately, in this stage of the revolutionary movement, we have encountered

extreme resistance. In terms of foreign relations, our country is subjected to increased oppression and is still in a semi-colonial status. In terms of domestic affairs, bandits have not been completely eliminated, which has dispersed our revolutionary forces. And foreign economic aggression, rural bankruptcy, and industrial and commercial decline have formed a serious economic national crisis. Our revolutionary movement has been hit by this. How can we break through the current difficulties? How can we solve this economic national crisis? This requires every revolutionary to use our knowledge to solve this problem. Let's look at the facts before us. As I said before, the current stage of the Chinese revolution is political tutelage and construction. The success or failure of this work completely depends on the level of knowledge of the people.

According to expert statistics, the Chinese illiterate population accounts for more than 70% of the total population. These illiterate people cannot even write their own names. How can we ask them to exercise the four powers? When it comes to construction, modern material construction must be based on science, but there is a lack of domestic talent. We have to rely on foreign technical experts. Foreign experts often do not fully understand our country's national conditions, and their plans may not be suitable for our needs. From this, we can learn a lesson: cultivating specialized talents and improving the national level of knowledge are prerequisites for completing the current stage of revolutionary work. Based on the above analysis, we can say that the reading movement has extremely important significance. The reading movement currently led by the Cultural Construction Association focuses more on promoting profound knowledge, rather than a widespread movement to eliminate illiteracy. This is because promoting profound knowledge is particularly important during the current construction period. We must cultivate

many talents and experts to engage in construction work. Dr. Sun Yat-sen said that the foundation of the revolution lies in profound knowledge. This is what he meant. Last year, the Japanese military published a booklet saying that future wars will be wars of the entire nation, wars of the intelligence of the people of both countries. It also stimulates people to engage in the pursuit of knowledge. In order to improve cultural standards, increase the national level of knowledge, and promote intellectual national defense, we must encourage the people to read and cultivate a good learning atmosphere among the people. We must encourage young people to devote themselves to academic studies and develop a national reading movement. This is a movement to relieve intellectual famine, a movement to cultivate national strength and change national destiny. As for the movement to eliminate illiteracy, in terms of

the central government, the Central Executive Committee has a three-year plan to eliminate illiteracy. In Shanghai, the municipal government has a People's Literacy Committee, which plans to eliminate all illiteracy in Shanghai within one year. The purpose of this movement to eliminate illiteracy is to raise the national level of knowledge and reduce the resistance to the revolution. If this national, unified promotion of the reading movement succeeds one day, when we talk about political tutelage and construction, we will inevitably be able to promote it without obstruction. Therefore, every one of our citizens should vigorously support and defend this movement. Finally, I respectfully wish the Cultural Construction Association's reading movement success, and I hope that the people of the whole country will work hard to promote the reading movement.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Fei Cun)

Only those who truly understand optimism have happiness; at the same time, only those who can truly cope with the environment have happiness. Although the environment in front of you is so bad, you should still know how to deal with the bad environment in front of you. Otherwise, what's the use of your daily sadness, moaning, and depression?

Many people are cursing the existing society, and some are even resentful of being born into the present society. How wrong is this! We should know, what is society? We should also understand, what is the composition of social organization? If we have a deep understanding of the entire society, at least the sins produced in society should be attributed to ourselves! (Fei Cun)

She People

— Shi Ming

The She people, also known as She Yao, were originally a branch of the Yao people, traditionally believed to be descendants of Pan Hu. Their ancestor is said to be a dragon dog. This myth is known to everyone in the She tribe. Who their ancestor really is, it is temporarily impossible to find any historical facts to break the fallacies in the legends. However, it can be determined that the Yao people migrated from Guangdong to Fujian, and from Fujian to Zhejiang.

The She people are divided into ten surnames: initially only the Pan, Lan, Lei, and Zhong surnames, later adding the Gou, Lou, Hu, and Hou surnames, and recently adding the Lin and Li families. Those who are distributed in the counties belonging to the old government of Quzhou in Zhejiang Province are mostly in Lishui and Suichang. It is estimated that there are 200,000 She people in Zhejiang. Those who are distributed in Fujian include Gutian, Changting, and other twenty counties. The number of people is unknown. In addition, there are also some She people in Hunan, Guangdong, and Yangyuan in Anhui.

Their marriage system is patrilineal, and they generally practice monogamy. Marriage within five generations is not allowed, and marriage is determined by the parents' orders and the matchmaker's words. However, their men and women are absolutely equal. Their funeral system is similar to that of the Han people, but when the deceased is put into the coffin, there is no wailing, but songs are sung instead. In the past, cremation was popular, but recently the burial methods of the Han people have gradually been adopted.

In the organization of the She people's families, whether men or women, they all have equal rights to enjoy the inheritance of property. They are rich in clan concepts and mostly live in clans. In the same community, there is a clan head in charge of rewards and punishments. Within the residential area, a covenant is established. If there is a violation of the rules, it must be punished after public discussion, and in severe cases, they are expelled from the area. However, they are strong in keeping faith, and violations of discipline are rarely seen.

The individual and social morality of the She people is better than that of the Han people. However, the Han people despise them very much. Therefore, there is a huge difference in the education and status of the She people. I hope the authorities will pay attention to this point.

Nodding Off

— Rong Yu

Nodding off is a very ordinary and trivial thing, but a careful study reveals that it also has some small value and interest.

The causes of nodding off are nothing more than "fatigue," "drowsiness," and "lack of energy"; and among them, there are distinctions of "climate," "constitution," and "habit": those related to climate generally nod off more easily in spring and summer than in autumn and winter, so there are ancient poems such as "Spring sleep unaware of dawn," "Lying high in the northern window, companions of Xi Huang," and "The summer sun is hot, just right for sleeping." Those related to constitution are generally easier for fat people to nod off than thin people. I don't know about the ancients, but just take the former military governor of Shaanxi, Hu Jingyi, as an example. His body was extraordinarily fat, and his skill in nodding off was also beyond the reach of ordinary people. He would even snore while sitting in the room talking to his staff. Those related to habit are generally lazy and comfortable people. Even if they get enough sleep at night, they are used to nodding off during the day, and they will fall asleep soundly at a certain time. In addition, there are special circumstances: such as lack of sleep at night, ...playing cards and drinking,... one will also nod off during the day; the shaking of boats and cars will also make people close their eyes and turn their heads to sleep.

Nodding off is not a good habit after all. I saw the ugly state of others nodding off in boats and cars, which made me afraid to try it myself. Some people's heads move with the bumps of the car, and their bodies also lean forward and backward. Sometimes, if one is not careful, one will fall to the ground, causing people to laugh out loud. Some people lie on their sides, limp, and fall on the body of a stranger, with saliva flowing an inch long, resulting in people hating them and scolding them severely.

"Where there is a will, iron can be made to blossom." To drive away this sleepy bug, you don't need spells or medicine, you just need to perk up your spirits, and it will retreat three times.

Little West Heaven

Chapter 11: Nighttime Talk of Tragic Life, Originally a Dream, Footprints Scattered, the Wind and Rain Are Too Deceiving

It is now the morning of the day, and everyone is energetic. The lingering emotions of last night, those tragic and entangled events, are probably all forgotten. Jia Duocai frowned and said, "This place in Xi'an is already boring enough. Adding to the rain, you can't even step out of the gate. How do you spend such long days?" Matchmaking is just a hope, what way is there to regulate boredom." Huanhua glanced at him and laughed, "There's always a way, it's not difficult..." After saying these eight words, she immediately realized that what she had said was too ambiguous, and blushed and said, "Mr. Li, don't laugh, I haven't finished speaking. I was thinking that if I go find that girl, I will definitely be able to do it. Mr. Jia, why don't you order some dishes and some wine, so that I can eat and be happy to go matchmaking, okay? Records of Fragrant Imperial Footwear

— Original by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

The room for storing these phoenix shoes was also a very large side hall. The walls on all sides, from the ceiling to the floor, were all made of wooden boards into many wooden boxes, hundreds of rows without exaggeration. Each pair of phoenix shoes occupied a box, and the outside was numbered in order. In addition, there was a very thick book, which also recorded the same numbers, and under each number, the style, color, pattern, etc. of the pair of phoenix shoes were clearly noted; this book was kept by a female official who specialized in writing documents for the Empress Dowager. When the Empress Dowager was suddenly happy and wanted to change a pair of phoenix shoes, she would instruct this female official to send the book up for her to look through slowly; after she had decided, she only needed to say a number, and someone could immediately be sent to fetch the pair of new shoes she had chosen. Now that I think about it, it can be regarded as a scientific management method suitable for the principle of time economy!

The two eunuchs who specialized in keeping the phoenix shoes, of course, could not be regarded as craftsmen in the shoemaking industry, but only as one of the executive personnel in the palace. The so-called craftsmen in the shoemaking industry were another group of people, and they were also women, but they did not work as palace maids and could come and go freely. The work they undertook was indeed a specialized skill, which could not be done by ordinary people without training, but it was not very hard; from my perspective as an observer, it was as fun and interesting as the work done by other craftsmen in the palace. Among them, there were also two leaders who were responsible for management, who were two old women in their fifties.——In fact, they were not old women, but old maids; they were hired into the palace when they were very young. (287)

Peach and Plum Calamity

— (Xia Hu)

Our Gan Nanbei Lake is surrounded by peach and plum trees. When the flowers bloom, the red clouds and white snow reflect each other, which is very interesting. This lake is famous for its peach blossoms, and can be directly named Peach Blossom Lake. In the spring of previous years, tourists flocked here, and the local farmers by the lake guided tourists to visit, making a little progress. This year, there are few tourists, and the ill-fated peach blossoms have suffered from wind, fog, frost, and snow. Before they bloom, they fall. Those who pass by only see desolation and the people look emaciated. According to the farmers, "If a hundred flowers are frosted, the harvest is disappointing!" Last year there was a drought, and the farmers hoped for a bumper harvest of broad beans, peas, flowers, and fruits this spring to slightly restore the damaged vitality. Now that the peach and plum trees have suffered a calamity and a hundred flowers have withered early, the people will see even greater difficulties.

World Strange News

Begging Art

— Huang Yingdai

Carrying Twelve Pounds in Gold

In London or other important cities in England, vagrants and beggars with artistic skills can sometimes be fortunate enough to accumulate a lot of property. Recently, a beggar was arrested by the police in the west of London for begging with twelve pounds of gold on him and was sentenced to three months' imprisonment. In court, the beggar complained that he was very poor and almost unable to make a living, so he begged. However, the judge later found twelve pounds of property on him and sentenced him to three months in prison and asked him to pay five pounds for living expenses while in prison.

Holding a Banquet After Death

William Stevenson was the famous "King of Scottish Beggars." When he was dying, he wrote a will to hold a grand banquet to entertain all the beggars with the art of begging, so that they could all come and kiss his remains while he was lying in state, so that he could die in peace. This grand banquet was truly amazing. A total of three warehouses were rented, and thirty sheep were slaughtered to serve as dishes for the guests. In addition, countless beers were consumed, and there were more than eight gallons of the best whiskey. It can be seen that this banquet cost a lot of money!

A Legacy of Three Thousand Pounds

Cha Aaron, this poor man was a famous beggar in London. He wore a very long fake beard on his face, and most people knew that he had not enjoyed sleeping in a bed for fifty years, in other words, he slept on the ground every day. But after he died, he left a legacy of three thousand pounds.

Son is a College Student

But here is an even more ingenious beggar named Tem France. He sent his son to Edinburgh University with the money he begged for. His begging method was to hold two pockets in his hand. If a kind gentleman put a coin into one of his pockets, he would pay attention to another and give the same alms, and he would say, "My son is studying at the university, please help him with some tuition!" It is also a very interesting thing for the father to beg and provide his son's tuition at the university, right? People will be happy to donate after hearing him without having to beg. Later, this young man once entered the cabinet, and when he died, he was already old. In England, this matter is still spread as a good story.

Donated a Huge Legacy

Banaeov Ning was a famous Irish beggar who begged for two thousand five hundred pounds in his lifetime. He wrote a will stating that after his death, he would use this huge amount of money to help the poor among his relatives and friends, but a pastor advised him to donate it to a charity in Rome, so he listened to the pastor and donated it all. Later, the church often talked about this beggar's great deed, saying that although he was dead, he was still glorious and worthy of it.

Financial Buying Interest Weakens, Gold Bidding Sellers Show Their Might, Down Eight Yuan Four - Retreating to Seventy Yuan

The gold market has been succumbing to selling pressure for consecutive days, and yesterday's market was no exception. Although the foreign exchange market did not loosen, the buying side of the gold market was weak, with no activity at all. Once there was a supply of funds, there was a lack of maintenance, and the result was very sluggish. In the early morning, the London and New York silver markets both rose, and the Menterie forward silver price also rose. The exchange rate did not fluctuate much, and the London spot gold rose by two and a half pence. People's hearts were tired, and the off-site pre-trading opened, slightly retreating to seventy-three or four yuan. Unexpectedly, the sellers were eager and lacked maintenance, and immediately fell. The Central Bank's official quotations were announced, with both the United States and the United Kingdom being flat, and the customs gold unit rose by three cents. The standard price of the gold bid rose to 900 yuan and 1 jiao, slightly turning steady. After the low opening in the morning, it broke the 70 yuan mark. However, because the banks took advantage of the cheap price to buy, the buying side took advantage of the low price to act, and there was a slight rebound. However, the domestic market was sluggish and there was still a fall. The HSBC Bank's official quotations were announced, with both the United States and the United Kingdom being flat, and the market situation turned mediocre. Buyers were once active and rebounded slightly, but the rise was only temporary. Soon it became a hover again, and there were few transactions. There was a lack of special changes for quite a long time. Unexpectedly, the central government closed again, and large households took advantage of the situation to slightly sell, lacking maintenance. The foreign exchange market also hardened accordingly. Under the observation of buyers, it broke the 70 yuan mark again. Although there was a small trading in the middle, the buying interest was sluggish and the trend was weak. The market fell again after the market opened, but the buying side was seen to be still inactive, so it was able to maintain. The initial report of the Indian silver rose by 2.4.3 anna, in a hovering state. After entering, the news of Sassoon wanting to buy a shilling again arose, and the foreign exchange market tightened once and rebounded. The second report of the Indian silver was flat, slightly stable. However, people's hearts could not last, so although it rose after entering, it still fell. Buyers did not dare to act rashly, and the market was tired again at the close. It was difficult for the market to cheer up all day. In the middle, the rumors of borrowing money helped the retail investors' selling pressure. Now I will record the market situation of the day.

The opening in the morning was 871 yuan and a half, a decrease of two yuan and a half from last Saturday. Da Decheng, Qingfa, Yongdafa, and Yong sold strips, falling to 69 yuan and 2 jiao. Observations on the Future of U.S. Wheat

A report from New China Foreign Company on the U.S. wheat situation states that winter wheat is now in the spring growth months, and the lack of moisture to date is very significant. The southwestern hard winter wheat belt is particularly at risk of drought. Although it is still too early to predict a wheat crop failure, the poor condition of winter wheat entering spring is undeniable.

In recent years, domestic supply in the United States has been drastically reduced. When the current crop year, which began in July 1935, started, U.S. wheat stocks will fall to the so-called "statistical norm or safe stock" level. Therefore, if there is another crop failure this year, it could have serious consequences. The current supply is clearly not excessive. If it were to be heavily depleted, it would be necessary to import bread wheat. The domestic supply situation in the United States is listed as follows:

Domestic Supply (Unit: 1 Million Bushels)

Crop Year July 1 Stocks Winter Wheat Spring Wheat Total Supply Consumption June 30 Stocks

1931-32 324 818 114 1,256 874 382

1932-33 382 476 268 1,126 740 386

1933-34 386 352 176 913 622 291

1934-35 291 401 96 788 ×655 ×133

× Estimated numbers

Crop production on the Great Plains west of the 100th meridian is entirely limited by moisture. Sufficient rainfall in late summer and autumn is the source of soil moisture supply. When wheat growth is most active and water is insufficient to meet its needs, seedlings absorb this moisture and rely on it for growth. Therefore, the large accumulation of subsoil moisture is related to wheat crops as savings are to a person's bank account. Rainfall in the U.S. hard winter wheat belt from July to the end of September last year was minimal.

Winter wheat planting starts from mid-September and continues until the end of November. During this period, abundant rainfall allows the seeds to germinate and the seedlings to establish. Well-rooted seedlings are more resistant to winter cold, wind, and soil changes than those that are not firmly rooted. From October 3 last year to February 26 this year, the western wheat-growing region has not received its normal moisture supply. In fact, most of the rainfall in the southwest is less than 50% of what it was during this period in previous years. Recent reports of severe dust storms indicate that there is still a lack of adequate moisture.

The situation in the eastern winter wheat belt is generally satisfactory, but the situation in the western region is quite different. Due to the lack of moisture in the subsoil, the future harvest will depend entirely on the weather from now until harvest time. For a bumper harvest, rainfall must be widespread and well distributed. According to estimates by Department of Agriculture officials, winter wheat on the western Great Plains requires 121% more moisture than normal from now until harvest time, and they say that there is only a 20% chance of this happening.

It is still too early to discuss the outlook for spring wheat, but we must point out that most spring wheat areas also lack adequate rainfall, resulting in lower than average subsoil moisture.

To achieve average production, rainfall in the coming months must be more than usual and timely. Last year's drought is still fresh in our memories. The supply of wheat this year is not only gradually decreasing, but this year's harvest will also face a confirmed threat. If the situation does not improve in the short term, the seeds of a crop panic will be sown for the coming months.

Due to Japanese business propaganda, the U.S. government is extremely discriminatory towards Chinese tea imports. The standards set are not the same as for tea from Java and Japan. Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Is This Kind of Abortion a Crime?

— Meng Ruo

Reading the social news in the Shen Bao on the 4th, I was struck by this passage: Shen Chen, from Zhenjiang, worked as a servant in the home of a Japanese resident in this city. Recently, she became pregnant for three months, and fearing that her abdomen would gradually expand, making it difficult to work, or that she might be fired by her employer, she privately inserted a raisin into her lower body to induce an abortion. After the incident, the court sentenced her to two years in prison for abortion, with a suspended sentence.

After reading this article, my heart jumped, and I felt that the pressure of livelihood was truly terrifying. If this young woman had been fortunate enough to marry a wealthy man, she would have been overjoyed to be pregnant. Perhaps she would give birth to a little baby, and the couple would have a source of comfort. Her in-laws would be beaming with smiles and cherish her even more. However, she was unfortunate. Because her family was poor, she had to work as a maidservant to earn a few dollars to support her life. Selling her labor is not a problem, but now even the flesh in her womb must be aborted due to the pressure of life. Although her life was saved thanks to God's blessing, she could not escape a two-year sentence. Her plight is truly pitiful.

Abortion is cruel from a humanitarian perspective and a crime from a legal perspective. However, humanity and law are sometimes no match for the whip of life. There are many poor people in the world who secretly engage in this cruel and criminal act.

Old Man Hu

— Hua Mu

In the evening, Old Man Hu listlessly crawled out of the cabin. The river was calm and peaceful, sprinkled with soft sunlight. He looked up at the clouds on the horizon, his heart feeling like a rock was stuffed inside, heavy and stagnant. He aimlessly touched the iron nail-like whiskers on his chin, shook his head blankly, as if saying: Another day is over.

He staggered ashore. Behind the mountain, there was a thunderous sound of a car running over the muddy road, raising a cloud of yellow dust. Strangely, this cloud of yellow dust was like spitting out from the mouth of a python, rolling over the sky and earth towards him, causing Old Man Hu to feel chills. "It's over, this old bone!" He sighed deeply and turned into the small tavern on the right side of the dock.

The tavern was cold and desolate, and the wine stove was listless on the side. When Old Man Hu saw this desolation, he felt another pang of sadness, as if being teased by a general pressure. He drank strong wine, and his brain clearly turned over the old events.

He remembered himself starting to travel to the market boat in his twenties. The Jiaotang dock was lively every evening. A row of boats stretched across the river, with the bow of one boat biting the stern of another, their bellies heavily loaded. As soon as the boat stopped, his companions would wipe their faces in the river, put on clean jackets, and climb ashore in groups of three or five, all carefree. But now it has changed. Since a highway was built behind the mountain, monster-like cars sped through the day, raising mud and dust half the sky high, carrying full loads of market customers and goods every day. In less than half a month, the Jiaotang dock had suddenly turned into a wasteland after a fire, desolate and bleak. Four out of five taverns had closed, and the one remaining was gasping feebly. Old Man Hu's boat had stopped running at this time, and he leaned against the banyan tree on the left side of the dock, drinking river water in misery...

This irreversible and fatal blow did not confuse Old Man Hu. He understood that it was the highway behind the mountain that was to blame, stealing his rice bowl. So he felt chills in his heart when he heard the sound of cars and saw the yellow dust?

It's over. This old bone!

Page 18

The days slipped by in despair. Life and sorrow turned into two red-hot iron needles, piercing through Old Man Hu's heart. Several times, he wanted to simply kill the heart of the market boat, sell the boat, go back to his hometown to farm, sip thin porridge, and muddle through the days. But this idea would turn into a bubble from time to time, rising quickly and then bursting. His heart could not help but soften. His family of six had only five ancestral grain shares of dry land. If it weren't for this boat, they would have starved to death long ago. How could they have survived to this day? Thinking of this difficult moment, Old Man Hu put the wine bowl on his lips and stared blankly at the calm river, as if using all his strength to grab something floating on the surface of the water...

The sun was gone. The river and the mountains gradually pulled down the blurred night shadows. Old Man Hu drank the last bowl of wine with a sore throat.

The days slipped by quietly with the river, one day, two days... Under the banyan tree at Jiaotang Dock was empty, without Old Man Hu's boat.

The Death of a Child

— Li Ni

Lin has been a little abnormal lately: She hasn't looked in the mirror for days, tidied her messy, tangled hair; nor does she put on powder and rouge on her face, which is yellow and frightening like wax! She lies in bed all day long, weeping, soaking the pillow with her tears.

Ren also paces back and forth in the room, dejectedly, with his hands behind his back. His face has no luster, as if covered with a layer of dust, or like someone who has insomnia and doesn't get enough sleep at night. He often stops in front of the bed, watching Lin's shoulders rise and fall quickly, and listening to the faint sobs from her throat. He sits down, gently strokes her tangled hair, and mumbles——

"Lin, are you feeling bad? ... Honey, just pretend it never happened, don't be sad! ... Actually, living in this world is also suffering. We can't even fill our stomachs, how can we ...; "Ren's throat is also hoarse, and his voice is low and trembling.

Lin cries even more vigorously, her shoulders twitching rapidly, and her whole body trembling faintly.

With one less child in the family, the air is particularly silent and still! Little Lin has only been dead for three or four days, and the room is as quiet as an ancient temple in the deep mountains. Everything is dim, without a bit of life.

Normally, when Ren returns home from outside, Lin, holding Little Lin, would greet him with a smiling face: "Little Lin, call daddy, daddy bought candy for you." Then, Little Lin would stretch out her little hands to ask for candy, calling out simple sounds. At that time, Ren was also extremely happy. He would take the child from Lin's arms, tease her, and teach her to speak, forgetting the burden on his shoulders, forgetting the idleness and humiliation he had suffered outside. He forgot all the pain, leaving it clean and pure, and he felt that the air in the family was warm and joyful.

"But Little Lin is already dead." He thinks: His head swings like a pendulum.

However, in order to prevent Lin from being overly sad, he had to put on a smile and calmly comfort her——

"Lin, take it easy, get up! Let's go out to eat together, and then find a fun place to go for a walk. ... We're still young, maybe we'll have three or five more in the future. ..."

Lin still refuses to get up, continuing to sob.

Finally, Ren stood up again, lowering his head, with his hands behind his back, dragging his heavy feet, pacing back and forth in front of the bed, feeling suffocated!

He remembers Little Lin's chubby face, lively black eyes, who would roll out of bed as soon as it was dawn, peel open his eyelids, caress Lin's hair, and call out, "Daddy, Mommy."

"How could this lively little life wither away so quickly? ..." He secretly thought. At the same time, a wave of shame rolled up from his stomach, suffocating his heart, making him so painful that he could not stand still, and everything in front of him was spinning rapidly. He murmured madly:

"I'm really not qualified to be a father, I'm too irresponsible to the child! Little Lin only caught a cold, and there was no money to hire a doctor for her, so she lay in bed and died quietly!" He angrily grabbed the hair on his head, completely mad, staggered to the bed, threw himself into Lin's arms, and cried with Lin to his heart's content. ...

Opening piece: "The Kitchen God Goes to War"

The Kitchen God emperor sits on the kitchen stove. He relies on the incense smoke to have divine power. The main hall, mountains, and rivers are all within the stove. His mighty spirit is extraordinarily prominent. Suddenly, a cockroach scout brings military intelligence: 100,000 red ants are invading. General Camel has already gone to block them. Their momentum is like splitting bamboo, their courage extraordinary. The stove door has been opened. The soup pipe river has been defeated and retreated. The enemy forces will arrive at Stove Mountain any day now. The Kitchen God hears this and is filled with unbearable anger. He says, "I must personally lead the troops on a campaign." He rolls up the stove curtain and comes out into the courtyard. He sits on a firewood stool, wearing a coin helmet. His left hand holds fire tongs, his right hand wields a wok handle. The two armies meet six feet in front of the stove. The stove brick waves form the ranks. A fierce battle ensues, with no victor. The Kitchen God quickly unleashes his magic weapon. He scatters a handful of stove ash from his robe sleeve, burying the red ants in the ash heap. The ants were about to use their pincers to clamp the Kitchen God, causing him unbearable pain. He cries out, "Who can save me?" Fortunately, the warmed-up stove cat leaps out and performs a meritorious service. It reorganizes the small Jiangshan [territory] of the entire stove.

Classical Prose

Wang Bingmei - "Donglai Bo Yi"

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Zang Aibo Admonishes Gao Ding (Continued): "The thief who breaks through the gate, people do not blame him for sneaking and peeping; the prisoner who kills someone, people do not blame him for fighting and brawling. To summarize sneaking and peeping with breaking through the gate is a minor matter. To summarize fighting and brawling with killing someone is a minor crime. Duke Huan personally committed regicide and was not censured; how can he be blamed for taking one tripod from a rebellious person? It is appropriate that his advice was not accepted." From the former statement, it is disloyal; from the latter statement, it is unwise. One instance of advice embodies two failures. People say Aibo is virtuous; I do not believe it. Alas, Yan You's plan for dealing with the Xiongnu was an extraordinary plan, but gentlemen do not call it extraordinary because he told it to Wang Mang. Chen Zi'ang's memorial to the Mingtang was a loyal memorial, but gentlemen do not call it loyal because he told it to Empress Wu. Zang Aibo's admonishment about Shao Ding was loyal advice, but gentlemen do not call it loyal because he told it to Duke Huan. When observing a person's words, one should first consider the place where they are, and then listen to the words they utter. If one loses oneself in a region of usurpation and rebellion, even if there are loyal words and excellent plans, they will inevitably aid in the chaos. If Duke Huan had used Aibo's words and consistently followed legal principles, adhering to the idea of taking by rebellion but governing by righteousness, then there would have been no disaster of Peng Sheng, and Duke Yin's eyes would never have been closed in the underworld. Is Aibo's crime not great? I once said that Yu Fu's request to write a plan for Duke Huan to usurp the state and Aibo's advice to build a plan for Duke Huan to protect the state: Yu Fu started the chaos, Aibo completed the chaos. In justly naming and defining crimes, Aibo should not be placed below Yu Fu.

Shenbao Local Supplement Movie Special

What Ziegfeld Considered Ugly Became Stars in the Film Industry (Part 1)

— Xin Ni

Florenz Ziegfeld, after his death, was given an honorific in the entertainment world, called "The Great Ziegfeld," and a film was made about his life and deeds, praising his entire career. Why? It was all because of his lifelong dedication to promoting beauty. All his life, he pursued perfection, etc. He was the Cellini of Broadway (Italian sculptor), except that he worked with female forms, while Cellini worked with metal.

Ziegfeld's revue was famous in the United States for decades, and the beautiful women who came out of it and entered the film world were countless. We can list a few famous ones, such as Lillian Tashman (deceased), Billie Dove, Dorothy Mackaill, Marion Davies, Mae Murray, etc., all of whom were promoted by the Great Ziegfeld.

But if Ziegfeld saw Greta Garbo, Katharine Hepburn, Janet Gaynor, Joan Crawford, Helen Hayes, Anna Sten, etc., who are now famous in the film world, would he choose them to join his revue? Everyone knows that it would be impossible. He would definitely tell his assistants, Ned Wayburn or Cholmley Gibb, to get them out quickly. As for why, he might talk to you about it when he was in a good mood, but Ziegfeld's temper was usually very volatile, and he wasn't very willing to talk about his reasons.

But in Ziegfeld's mind, what kind of person was Greta Garbo? He would definitely say that her mouth was facing this way, and her eyes were facing that way. He would also say that her forehead was too high and her nose was too low. He might say that her eye sockets were too deep and her upper lip drooped too much. These are the words of an artist, and that is, the words of Ziegfeld. But no matter what, Greta Garbo is a beauty with a unique charm on the screen.

If Katharine Hepburn went to Ziegfeld looking for a job, Ziegfeld would look at her and say, "No, no," and chase her away. If Katharine insisted on knowing why, and Ziegfeld was willing to talk to her for a minute or two, he would tell her that her cheekbones were too high, her cheekbones were too long, and her entire face looked too much like someone from the Stone Age: In short, her face was a horse face. But Katharine still retains her beauty on the screen, and her beauty is based on her flaws.

Ziegfeld's life's work was measuring beauty with a ruler. He established an immutable standard for perfect beauty in dimensions. For example, "The height must be five feet five inches (English), bust thirty-four inches, waist twenty-six inches, hips thirty-seven inches, calf thirteen and a half inches, shoulder circumference fifteen inches, neck to waist fifteen inches, neck length two and a half inches, arm length twenty-seven inches, etc." But...

We don't want to pry into the secrets of the makeup rooms of the major stars, but it is clear that very few of them meet Ziegfeld's dimensions of beauty. For example, comparing Greta Garbo to Janet Gaynor, Garbo is six inches taller than Gaynor, and Gaynor weighs twenty-six pounds less than Garbo. Neither of them meets the standard of beauty, but both of them occupy the highest position on the screen, coexisting without interfering with each other. (To be continued)

Movie Reviews

"The Iron Hand of Compassion"

— Zhao Ren

Father Brown, Detective — Cathay Release

About a month or so ago, I saw a movie, the title of which I have already forgotten. I only remember that the story was about a famous playwright who bravely saved the lives of several women when a ship was wrecked. The women he saved were naturally very grateful, but thinking that he had died, they erected a bronze statue in front of his theater to commemorate him. So, his wife, children, and family all thought he was dead and were very sad. Who knew that in the crisis, he cowardly escaped in women's clothing. Although he saved his life, he felt infinite shame. Especially because people praised him as a hero, he was even more embarrassed to go home and had to change his name and wander. More than ten years later, missing his wife, he secretly returned home, but he did not dare to meet his wife. He secretly helped his son, whom he did not know, succeed in theater. Finally, he met his wife and began to live a wandering life again.

This drama has a strong sense of sadness and deep human sentiment, which greatly moved me. The performance of the lead actor, Walter Connolly, was also a great success. Because of this, I paid close attention to this actor. However, I do not praise "The Iron Hand of Compassion," which he starred in this time.

First of all, I don't like this kind of story, which combines religion and politics, using the power of religious influence to make criminals reform and do good. Using this empty sermon as the theme of the play, in the era of scientific prosperity in the twentieth century, it is not the work of a wise man, no matter how the playwright handles the work, right? No one will ignore the playwright's intentions. He uses film art as an aid to politics, which is naturally beneficial to those in power. However, people will not ignore the behavior of thieves, which is the sin of society. People cannot point out the pathology of society from its essence, and then inspire the audience to transform society, but only painstakingly maintain the crumbling social existence, which is just hard work in vain. In fact, American criminals will not be eliminated or reduced because of religious preaching.

Even in terms of expression techniques, it cannot clearly convey the theme of the play and the intentions of the playwright. On the contrary, in order to exaggerate Father Brown's holiness too much, people think that he is just a fictional character in mythology and has an aura of unreality. Of course, this is not without successful performances. For example, the entire play can proceed in a tranquil atmosphere, and the solemn and solemn mood is full of the film. The scenes of individual psychological descriptions, such as when the uncle of the girl is worried about the theft, are also handled well. But overall, most of it can be said to be unsuccessful. And the performance of the lead actor, Walter Connolly, does not show his excellence.

However, I also feel that in this film, it is superfluous to only point out the failure in terms of technology. Because vulgar content can only have vulgar expression.

A Story of Joan Crawford Before She Became Famous

— Guo Cheng

The following is a story about Joan Crawford joining the chorus before she became famous on the screen.

When Joan Crawford was in high school, she was a little girl who was very good at pleasing people. Among all the students, she was also famous for her dancing skills. Whenever she thought about her future, she would think of things about singing and dancing; this was because singing and dancing gave her too much interest. One day, she suddenly made a firm decision, left school the next day, and ran to her mother in Kansas City, preparing to find a job. The main purpose of her working was to save some money so that she could participate in the singing and dancing business.

So, she worked as a clerk in a store. On the one hand, she saved money, and on the other hand, she used the money to buy some new clothes. Later, she heard that a theater manager in the western region was recruiting young girls to be temporary chorus performers, so she immediately ran to apply. It turned out that it was a singing and dancing performance group in Springfield. When she arrived at Springfield, she changed her pseudonym to Lucilke Le Sueur, which was her mother's name in her maiden days.

But this time, she only participated in this chorus group for a very short period of time. She was only employed for two weeks. The remuneration she received was only enough for her to return to Kansas City. However, these two weeks of life enhanced her interest in participating in that business.

Later, she felt that there seemed to be no hope in Kansas City, so she took the train to Chicago. All she brought with her were two silver dollars and a high degree of hope. She searched everywhere for a position as a member of a chorus group, but it was not easy in this foreign city. Finally, she ran to Ernie Young, because she had heard someone say that Ernie Young was a theater owner.

It was a strange and coincidental thing that on this day, the "Chicago Cafe" was holding a grand singing concert, and Ernie Young allowed her to join as a temporary member in this concert.

In the following eight weeks, she was promoted from the inconspicuous third row to the end of the first row (this refers to the arrangement of the singing group, people who sing well stand in the first row), although she still had not been formally employed at this time.

That night, the theater was rehearsing a new singing and dancing comedy, "Innocent Eyes." Joan Crawford was also dancing, showing a very novel style and posture. The theater owner saw this at this time and agreed to give her a formal employment position.

Her position was assigned to the "Ponies" group, where many young girls treated her very kindly. They helped her with makeup and taught her many new dance steps. Joan Crawford gradually developed from then on.

Gong Jianong Causes Trouble and Goes to Jail

Old Gong Jianong is a man of upright character. Recently, he fell in love with the village girl A Xuan. They love each other and are already like husband and wife. Unexpectedly, A Xuan joined a fashion company as a female worker and was noticed by the pattern maker Wang Nanwen, who wanted her to be a performer in the fashion show. On the one hand, Wang Nanwen pursued her desperately, making a village girl who had just set foot in society unable to stop her mind from drifting. The night before the fashion show was held, various newspapers published photos of A Xuan's enchanting dress. When Old Gong saw it, he was furious and full of resentment. He warned A Xuan at the time, telling her not to participate, but A Xuan did not listen. So, the fashion show opened the next day. When A Xuan took the stage, Jianong suddenly broke in, tearing A Xuan's fashion to shreds. The pattern maker Wang Nanwen was also injured. As a result, he had to be arrested and imprisoned. -- Naturally, the above-mentioned facts are due to a reason, and there is no evidence to verify it. It is just a plot in "Falling Flowers Season."

Movie Novel

Amateur Reporter (After Office Hours) (5)

— Tong Yun

Sharon giggled and said, "Let them go. They'll come out when they're hungry." But Jim didn't listen; he knelt on the ground, searching. After a while, Sharon also knelt down. They both crawled under the sofa, looking for the fruit. Suddenly, the phone rang, and Sharon got up to answer it. It turned out to be Jim's call. After finishing the call, Jim told Sharon, "Tomorrow night is the opening night of the Riverside Club again. It's bound to be lively. Let's have dinner there tomorrow." Sharon looked at Jim's face with a puzzled expression and asked, "Is this an invitation or an assignment?" Jim thought for a moment and said, "It's an assignment." After a while, Mrs. Talbot brought in coffee, and they dispersed after having coffee.

The next evening, Jim and Sharon sat facing each other, having dinner at the Riverside Club. Jim leaned closer to Sharon and asked, "If I hadn't said it was an assignment when I asked you yesterday, but said it was an invitation, would you still have agreed to come?" Sharon pretended to be looking at the menu, but she couldn't see a single word clearly. When she heard Jim ask her a question, she looked up and replied, "I would have come, but I would have thanked you." Jim inadvertently admitted, "I'm a bit timid; I was afraid you wouldn't come, so I had to say it was an assignment."

Jim was usually very good at telling jokes and making people laugh, but today, he seemed to have something on his mind and felt a bit restrained. After a while, he said, "Let's go for a walk outside. If you want to write about this club, you need to know everything about it." So they stood up and walked outside to stroll on the grassy area by the river. They intentionally walked a bit apart, but every few steps, they would naturally get closer and huddle together. They felt that there was a kind of attraction between them that constantly drew them together. Jim said, "I didn't expect tonight to be so beautiful." Sharon said, "I know... I know..." She couldn't say anything else.

Unconsciously, they had already reached the end of the grassy area, away from the noisy area. In the dimness, they became two dark shadows, standing side by side in the hazy light. Later, the two dark shadows gradually merged into one. Jim put his arm around Sharon and whispered, "Sharon, I love you, my darling." Sharon also whispered, "Jim?" He kissed her hair, soft, smooth, and sweet-smelling. After a while, he picked up her hand and kissed it. After they had been affectionate for a while, they slowly strolled back.

By this time, the room was already crowded with people. Among them were Patterson and his wife, sitting together. Inevitably, Tom Pannisdale was also there. When Sharon saw them, her hand trembled slightly as she reached for a cigarette. She seemed about to say something, and she stammered. Finally, she said angrily, "You knew Tom Pannisdale was coming today, coming with Julia Patterson, so you called me here, didn't you? You don't want to be with me. You just want me to watch them so I can write a news story for you!" Jim frankly admitted, "That's right, that was my original intention. But I had forgotten all about it until you reminded me."

Before he could finish speaking, Sharon had already stood up and said, "Oh, I see. A news reporter looking for news doesn't need to involve love affairs. I'm sorry, I'm going back." Pannisdale had already walked over by this time. He said to Sharon, "Hello, what a coincidence, I see you again." Sharon said, "Indeed, I was just looking for you." A waiter came over and said, "There's a phone call outside for Mr. Brown." Jim had no choice but to walk away to answer the phone. (To be continued)
